Current Affairs Commentary

After the American Gold Clause Case Verdict

— Li

The American gold clause case. Ever since the Washington Supreme Court accepted the trial on January 8th. The whole country, both government and the public, have paid extremely close attention. Because the Supreme Court's ruling on this case. Could influence Roosevelt's monetary policy. And this monetary policy is also the main part of the recovery movement. Observing that the Supreme Court did not make a ruling after the debate ended on January 11th. And the government urgently prepared countermeasures before the verdict. To prevent the verdict from being unfavorable to the government. It can be seen that this lawsuit is of great importance. Now this lawsuit has been formally ruled by the Supreme Court the day before yesterday (February 18th). The verdict is divided into two parts. The first is to acknowledge that the gold clause on private bonds is invalid. The second, although it acknowledges that government debts must still be fulfilled according to the gold clause. But if the government does not fulfill it. The creditor may not sue the government in court. To recover losses.

If we want to understand the implications of this case. We must first understand the course of this case. And where its importance lies. Tracing back to 1816, American public and private bonds all included a clause. Stipulating that when repaying debts, gold coins should be used, or other currency with a value equal to gold coins. This is the origin of the gold clause. This kind of provision. Can make the original rights and obligations between creditors and debtors. Not affected by changes in currency value. This provision has been in use for many years. Has become a convention. When President Roosevelt took office in 1933. Just as the United States was experiencing a financial panic. The Congress, in order to relieve the crisis. And to reform the finances. Therefore, on April 19th of that year, it announced the suspension of the gold standard. At the same time, the provisions of the gold clause. Also declared invalid. On June 5th, after President Roosevelt's signature. Became a law. After the gold clause was abolished. Domestic public opinion. Criticisms arose. Some even thought it was unconstitutional. Because it is contrary to the spirit of American law prohibiting states from using legislation to change contractual obligations. On January 31st, 1934. The government issued a currency devaluation decree. Reducing the weight of the U.S. dollar from 25.8 grams to 15 and 21/100 grams. That is, one new U.S. dollar and sixty-nine cents is only worth one old U.S. dollar. According to the provisions of these two laws. The losses suffered by American creditors are extremely significant. The gold clause case was a fierce opposition from creditors who suffered such losses. The plaintiff in this case. Is Norman, a bondholder of the Baltimore and Ohio Railroad Company. The defendant is the railroad company. On February 1st, 1930. The plaintiff purchased $1,000 in bonds from the defendant. Interest rate of 4.5%. Paid every six months. And with a gold clause attached. Norman duly requested interest from the defendant on February 1st, 1934. The defendant refused to fulfill the gold clause on the grounds of the laws of June 5th, 1933, and January 31st, 1934. Leading to litigation in the New York court. The plaintiff lost the case. So appealed to the Supreme Court. At the same time, there were three other similar lawsuits filed with the Supreme Court. All arising from this law. Seeking justice from the Supreme Court.

Legally speaking. The government's abolition of the gold clause law. Not only is it suspected of being unconstitutional. It also denies the gold standard law of 1900. The Second Liberty Bond Act. And all laws concerning the issuance of public bonds. Because these laws all recognize the gold clause. Before the verdict was announced. Everyone believed that the Supreme Court would act in accordance with the spirit of judicial independence. To protect the interests of creditors. Issuing a ruling unfavorable to the government. Observing that European countries were competing to sell off pounds and francs. Buying U.S. dollars. And the Chief Justice of the U.S. Supreme Court, Hughes, during the hearing of the case on January 8th. Also said, "Where did the government get the authority to change the gold repayment of freedom public debt?". The aspirations of the people. Can be seen here.

Finally, we should have a clear understanding of the impact of the Supreme Court's verdict on the United States and the world. The London exchange market has reversed. Those who were selling francs and pounds to buy U.S. dollars. All reversed their previous state. The price of the franc against the U.S. dollar. Rose sharply. And in the New York market. Stock prices have soared. This situation. Some may see it as a gain from Roosevelt's currency devaluation policy. Not knowing that this is the opportunism of speculators. Caused by this. Not the market activity caused by the devaluation of the U.S. dollar.

If we talk about the impact of international lending relations. Then China and other debtor countries that owe U.S. debt. If this verdict is cited. To repay the old U.S. debts with the already devalued U.S. dollars. The United States will suffer a major loss. I don't know if the U.S. government is willing to accept this loss. Or have other countermeasures. This is also a noteworthy issue.

All Staff of the Jiangxi Campaign Headquarters Go to Wuhan

Wuchang Campaign Headquarters Scheduled to be Established

[Nanchang] The Wuchang Campaign Headquarters is scheduled to be established on March 1st. All the staff of the former Nanchang Campaign Headquarters waiting for orders in Jiangxi, together with their families, totaling about 300 to 400 people, departed in two groups by special train from the province to Xunyang and then to Wuhan at 3:00 PM and 4:00 PM on the 20th. In order to encourage the staff to continue their efforts, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek specially summoned all the personnel at the original site of the Campaign Headquarters at 11:00 AM on the 20th and gave a sincere speech for half an hour. After lunch, all the personnel went to cross the river to prepare for departure. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek originally planned to fly to Wuhan. Both the Ford and Sikorsky aircraft were prepared and waiting for orders, and Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's luggage was also loaded onto the plane. However, as late as 2:00 PM, the weather in Nanchang was still gloomy, and Wuhan reported heavy rain by telegram. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek then temporarily changed his flight plan. All sectors of Jiangxi felt reluctant to say goodbye because the Campaign Headquarters had been established for five years and was finally able to completely eliminate the Red bandits, allowing the people of Jiangxi to live and work in peace. Various agencies, schools, and mass organizations went to cross the river to bid farewell, totaling no less than several thousand people. Xiong Shihui, Gu Zhutong, and the commissioners of the provincial government, Lü Xian, Gong Xuesui, Wu Jiantao, Cheng Shiying, Xiao Chunjin, and senior military and police generals Han Deqin, Lai Weiying, Huang Guangdou, etc., were all at the Niuxing Railway Station to see them off. The senior personnel who departed with the train included Secretary-General Yang Yongtai, Division Chiefs Yan Xunfu, Yan Daogang, Cai Jinjun, Secretaries Mao Qingxiang, Wang Rizhang, Chen Fang, and Section Chiefs and Guards, etc. It is expected that they will arrive in Xunyang one after another at 7:00 PM or 8:00 PM on the 20th. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek Issues a Letter to Compatriots Nationwide

In Commemoration of the New Life Movement's Anniversary

[Nanchang] Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, in commemoration of the anniversary of the New Life Movement, issued a letter of respect to compatriots nationwide. The original text is as follows: "The New Life Movement is actually the foundation of a new life for our Republic of China. Its purpose is to establish the rules of daily life, food, clothing, housing, and transportation for the people with the inherent virtues of our nation, namely propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame. It aims to promote inner construction through external training. This is an extremely ordinary movement, and it is also an effective remedy for the current environment and state of illness of our nation. Since it was initiated in Nanchang on February 19th of last year, it has been a year to this day. In order to review the past, encourage the future, and achieve the above-mentioned goals, I would like to reiterate its main points and point out the path for continued efforts, so as to encourage all my compatriots nationwide. When this movement was initiated last year, due to the eagerness of our people to seek national rejuvenation, the whole country responded and various places followed suit. The speed of progress was unprecedented. However, because the initial organizations in various places were diverse, the theories were not entirely the same, and the methods of promoting the movement were even more divergent and unfocused, lacking any standards, the Outline of the New Life Movement was formulated in May to explain the meaning in detail and stipulate the procedures. The New Life Movement General Association was established in Nanchang on July 1st, stipulating the organizational outline, reorganizing the New Life Movement associations in various places across the country, and showing the norms for progress, gradually advancing in stages, step by step, starting from oneself and extending to others, from the shallow to the deep, from things that do not cost money, time, or effort, and then to the rest, starting from organs, groups, schools, and public places, and gradually extending to the entire society, first using the two items of order and cleanliness as the central work of the first phase of the movement. Thus, from a state of free development, it progressed to a path of neatness and uniformity. Looking back on this year, although the achievements and progress in various places across the country have not been able to fully meet our expectations, fortunately, thanks to the unanimous respect and vigorous efforts of all virtuous people and compatriots nationwide, the perception of this movement, the awareness of order and cleanliness, has been able to penetrate into the hearts of the people, gradually forming a trend and creating a considerable foundation. This is indeed something that can be cited as infinite comfort. However, the effort devoted to the two items of order and cleanliness is only the preliminary work of this movement, hoping to use this as a starting point to correct the outdated life methods of our people. Now, in order to adapt to the needs of our nation and develop the life of our nation, it is essential to go a step further and realize the three major principles of militarization, productionalization, and artisticization shown in the new connection outline in the entire daily life of our compatriots, otherwise it will be in vain. The so-called militarization is not to arm all our compatriots and go to the frontiers together, but only to hope that they will emphasize organization, unity, strict discipline, order, know how to be invigorated, and maintain seriousness, so as to wash away the previous habits of disorder, romance, shirking responsibility, following conventions, and seeking temporary comfort. The so-called productionalization of life is not to have all our compatriots become farmers or workers, or to be engaged in commerce, but only to hope that all our compatriots can be thrifty, hardworking, mindful of the difficulty of material resources, and self-reliant in order to engage in the path of labor production, so as to wash away the previous habits of extravagance, waste, laziness, wandering, and greed. The so-called artisticization is not to have all our compatriots imitate the actions of poets, hackers, painters, and musicians, but only to hope that their personal conduct, dealings with others, and handling of affairs can be solemn, respectful, orderly, clean, lively, humble, quick, and reliable, so as to wash away the previous habits of crudeness, vulgarity, narrowness, ignorance, frivolity, and hypocrisy. If the above-mentioned three principles can be practiced and implemented one by one, and diligently learned without changing, then the four conditions of "propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame" will be fully met. If the life of one person is like this, then that person will surely be diligent and promising. If the life of one nation is like this, then that country will surely be rich, strong, and prosperous. Now, in order to enable all my compatriots nationwide to realize the spirit of these three types of life, the specific methods are: first, the training and organization of the people should be implemented; second, the organization of social cooperative undertakings should be promoted; and third, the popularization of various social educations should be intensified. All those in various places who are responsible for advocating the New Life Movement should immediately organize labor service groups separately, formulate plans properly according to the above methods, go deep into the people, and work hard to guide them. The organization of these service groups should be based on public officials, school teachers and students, and leaders of various industries, using their spare time, class breaks, after-work hours, or other holidays to engage in work, be the first to labor, be self-strengthening, and never slacken. Taking on the responsibility of educating and transforming the people, the New Life Movement will be more practical and will also be in line with the original intention of progressing from the shallow to the deep, from oneself and extending to others. The foundation of our revitalized nation will naturally be consolidated from this. Compatriots and gentlemen, please strive together! Chiang Chung-cheng, February 19th (Central News Agency dispatch on the 20th)

The Course of the Murder of American Missionary Mr. and Mrs. Standahl

The Magistrate of Jingde County Gave a Warning in Advance

Four Murderous Bandits Have Been Executed on the Spot

[Nanjing] The details of the murder of American missionary Mr. and Mrs. Standahl in Jingde, Anhui, have been published in various Chinese and foreign newspapers in Beijing and Shanghai, but the details are fragmented and not detailed, and there are some inaccuracies. Here is a reliable message obtained from relevant parties, which is recorded as follows: Jingde is located in a remote area of ​​southern Anhui, adjacent to the borders of Jiangxi and Zhejiang, in the midst of towering mountains and ridges. The transportation is extremely inconvenient, and there are no telegrams or telephones to transmit news. The communist bandits who broke through from Jiangxi and fled north first fled to Changhua, Zhejiang, and were defeated by the national army. As a result, they fled back to southern Anhui, and after being blocked by the central army everywhere, they detoured to attack Jingde in an attempt to flee north. Jingde had no people's self-defense forces, and because it happened suddenly, the few were no match for the many, so it fell on December 6th of last year. However, the national army attacked and suppressed the enemy step by step. The day of the fall was the day the county town was recovered by the pursuing army. Later, it was learned that an American missionary had been captured. In order to do its best to rescue foreigners, it advanced at an accelerated pace and pursued the enemy to Miaoshou. After a fierce battle for four hours, the communist bandits were finally driven back. Unfortunately, the missionary couple had already been killed at that time. After the Red bandits withdrew from Miaoshou, a fellow Christian, Luo Kezhou, ventured to go there on the 9th and found the remains of Mr. and Mrs. Standahl. He immediately joined the bandit suppression officials and the local Lianbao director to purchase good coffins for burial, and rescued the Standahl's daughter at the home of Wang Baozhang in the area. Later, she was sent to Jinan to be raised in the home of Shi Jinchen, the father of Mrs. Standahl. When Missionary Standahl arrived in Jingde in September of last year, Peng Shuhuang, the magistrate of the county, had told him that although Jingde was currently peaceful, communist bandits from the neighboring Huizhou area and Chunsu and other places in Zhejiang often came to harass them, and advised him to wait until next spring to come again. However, Missionary Standahl was enthusiastic about preaching, so he returned to Wu and brought his family to Jingde. The local officials then told him that he could only stay in Jingde temporarily, and that he would be notified in advance if there was any police news. On the morning of December 6th, at 6:00 AM, the communist bandits fled to Yangxi Station. At 7:00 AM, Magistrate Peng sent Zhang Zuwu, Chairman of the South Association, to the Gospel Church to instruct the Standahl couple to leave the country immediately. At about 8:00 AM, he sent He Gaoxuan, the quartermaster of the security team, to urge them to leave quickly. The protection was not inconsiderate. However, the missionary was determined to preach and did not want to break his promise to his fellow Christians, so he delayed his departure and eventually met with disaster. Later, the national army continued to pursue the enemy and the communist bandits in southern Anhui were investigated for the murderers. On December 14th, Wang Yaowu's brigade pursued the enemy to Tanjiabiao and engaged in a fierce battle all day, killing more than 400 bandits and capturing more than 100 bandits. The captured bandits were interrogated one by one, and Nan Aifeng, Jiang Bingfu, Zhu Maotou, and Hong Sanyuan confessed that they had participated in the murder of the American missionary couple in Miaoshou. After being interrogated by the Military Law Office of the Anhui Provincial Government Chairman's Office, it was confirmed that they were the murderers in this case and sentenced to death. They were executed on the spot on the 22nd to serve as a warning. It is heard that about 40 local officials and people were killed in the fall of Jingde this time, and dozens more were kidnapped. At that time, Peng Shuhuang, the magistrate of Jingde County, was dismissed and replaced by another person because the provincial government held him responsible for protecting the local area, even though the transportation was inconvenient, the bandits were numerous, and he was caught off guard. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 20th)

National Treasury Revenue Increases Sharply After Post Offices Sell Stamp Tax Tickets on Behalf

More Than Doubled in Peiping

[Nanjing] It has been three months since the financial authorities changed to selling new pagoda-style stamp tax tickets through post offices in various places. A Central News Agency reporter asked a responsible person from the Ministry of Finance on the 20th to inquire about everything to see what the benefits and harms of implementing this new system are. According to reports, the results obtained since the trial implementation, except for the number of tickets sold in remote provinces which decreased, all other provinces have increased compared to before, especially in various cities, which have increased by more than double. For example, in Peiping, the monthly average was more than 17,000 yuan, which increased to more than 28,000 yuan in November of last year, and increased to more than 39,000 yuan in December. The average monthly sales for the two months was more than 34,000 yuan. In addition, the average monthly sales of tickets in the ten provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, Fujian, Hubei, Henan, Shandong, Hebei, and Chahar, and the four cities of Beijing, Shanghai, Peiping, and Qingdao, was more than 580,000 yuan. In November, the total sales were more than 515,000 yuan, and in December, it was more than 534,000 yuan. Although it decreased by more than 50,000 yuan, the previous stamp tax bureau spent 20% of the total income, and the national treasury actually received only more than 470,000 yuan. Now, the post office sells on behalf, and the handling fee is only 6%. Based on the average for November and December, the national treasury can actually receive more than 490,000 yuan per month, an increase of more than 20,000 yuan compared to before. Such results were achieved at the beginning of the implementation of the new method. In the future, everything will be on track, and the tax revenue is expected to increase further. The reasons for this are: one is that the provinces and counties are conducting serious inspections, and the other is that the previous practice of forced apportionment has been abolished. As for the remote provinces, the commercial depression and the number of tickets sold are not large. In short, under the old system, the national treasury's income from ticket sales was not much, and the innocent losses suffered by merchants and people were very large. After the implementation of the new system, the national treasury's tax revenue has increased and the burden on the people has been greatly reduced. This has been achieved in terms of administrative efficiency, and the future is optimistic. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 20th)

US Increases Defense Spending to Build Invincible Air Force

Chairman of the House Land Committee Suggests

[Washington] The House Appropriations Committee continued to release the government's massive defense plan today and has reported on the unprecedented military budget proposed by the Army Department. According to the committee, the total amount of this budget reaches US$378,699,488, part of which is for the purchase of 547 Army aircraft, but this number is only the starting point for creating the world's largest air force. Today, Representative McSwain, Chairman of the House Army Committee, proposed a five-year aviation construction plan, McSwain visited the White House and then said that his proposal was to add 4,000 Army aircraft and 2,200 Navy aircraft. In addition, the Army Department's military supplies case also requires an increase in the strength of the National Guard and an expansion of the number of its official troops from 128,750 to 165,000. (National Telegram on the 19th)

The Army Department will have $318,000,000 in funding within the year ending June 1936, an increase of $48,000,000 compared to 1935. The committee stated today that if President Roosevelt increases the number of troops from 118,000 to 165,000, the Appropriations Committee is willing to continue raising Army funds. The current air force expenditure reaches $45,000,000, an increase of $19,000,000 compared to last year. (Reuters dispatch on the 19th)

Among the trainees are two imperial family members, Prince Fushimi-no-miya Tsuneyoshi and Prince Asaka-no-miya Yasuhiko, as well as the sons of General Kato, General Suetsugu, General Hyakutake, and Rear Admiral Nakamura. Diverse Opinions Among Countries on the Regulation of Arms Trade

[Geneva] The Arms Manufacturing and Trade Management Committee of the League of Nations Disarmament Conference met again today, but the opinions of the delegations from various countries are still far apart and difficult to reconcile. Therefore, at today's public meeting, the Polish representative, who was an investigator on this issue, immediately stood up and reported that after direct negotiations with various delegations, he has not yet been able to formulate any specific method to serve as a basis for continued discussion. Later, the General Assembly resolved to study the draft agreement proposed by the United States on a case-by-case basis. During the debate, it was discovered that on the issue of arms imports and exports, France intends to treat civilian aircraft and their parts as the same as military aircraft, while the United States argues that there should be a distinction between the United States and continental Europe on this point. In addition, the intention of the United Kingdom is to formulate a more complete list of categories beyond those listed in the US draft. The opinion of the Soviet representative is even more advanced than that expressed by France, not only should aircraft parts be regarded as military supplies, but all raw materials for manufacturing chemical warfare and gunpowder, such as sulfur, should also be included in military supplies. (National Telegram on the 19th)

Anglo-French Talks Again, London Agreement To Be Upheld

Suggestions Are Interrelated

Complete Consensus Between the Two Countries

[London] According to reliable sources, although the negotiations evoked by the London Declaration are a major topic in today's cabinet meeting, a definite resolution may not be clear by the end of this week. However, the second step is bound to be another joint note issued by Britain and France, acknowledging that Britain and Germany can negotiate directly, but the issues discussed should not be limited to the Air Pact, but should cover all agreements in the London Declaration. The press here believes that Simon seems to have the possibility of going to Berlin. (National Telegram on the 20th)

[London] Germany's reply to the suggestions jointly put forward by Britain and France supports the conclusion of a treaty by the major European countries. The British cabinet will also meet tomorrow to consider it, and then the two countries will exchange views. It is generally believed that although the British and French authorities believe that the Air Pact is an issue that must be discussed immediately, they do not think it appropriate to only stipulate that agreement while disregarding the other sections mentioned in the suggestions. (Reuters dispatch on the 19th)

British Cabinet Studies German Reply

[Paris] The Joint Committee of various departments of the British Cabinet on disarmament issues held a meeting to review the German reply of February 17. It was believed that the various suggestions contained in the Anglo-French London Declaration of February 3 are interconnected with each other and form a whole problem. The countries concerned should not focus on one point while ignoring the other points. This view is completely in line with the French government's opinion. Therefore, what Britain and France should reply to Germany before Britain and Germany conduct talks, the content has already been agreed, and what has not been decided is only a matter of form, and the secondary issue is whether the reply should be made jointly by the two countries, or only state that the letter has been received. It is heard that British Foreign Secretary Simon will come here before the 20th of this month to meet with Foreign Minister Laval, at which time a decision will surely be made. It seems that Britain and France will delay until the beginning of March to reply to Germany, and the meeting of British and German dignitaries will also be postponed until after Foreign Secretary Simon visits France. (Havas dispatch on the 20th)

British Newspapers Express Opinions

[London] The Times made some suggestions regarding the implementation procedure of the Anglo-French London proposal of February 3, roughly saying that we can negotiate with Germany on the Air Pact as much as possible, but we must wait for other issues (referring to Germany's return to the League of Nations, general disarmament treaty, Eastern European mutual assistance treaty, and Danube River treaty) to obtain the consent of the countries concerned before signing. For the current plan, it is appropriate to start re-establishing partial compromises in order to gradually realize the entire compromise. The overall relief plan cannot be accomplished overnight. The best way is for Britain to send someone to Berlin. Germany has the right to demand "equal negotiations" and will eventually get equal negotiations. Rather than letting Germany repeatedly demand concessions and other countries reluctantly making concessions, why not directly allow it with a friendly attitude? The News Chronicle believes that the Soviet Union and the Little Entente countries are very concerned about the Eastern European mutual assistance treaty and are very willing to see it established. It agrees with The Times that it should negotiate directly with Germany, because Germany's return to Geneva is a major issue. The Daily Herald also holds the same view, saying that if the Anglo-French plan is to succeed, all parties must negotiate freely on an equal footing. If each country or a certain group of countries puts forward conditions and forces people to recognize them, then the entire plan will inevitably be in danger. (Havas dispatch on the 20th)

Laval Attends Cabinet Meeting to Report on Anglo-French Talks

[Paris] Today, Foreign Minister Laval reported at the State Council the situation of the continued talks between Britain and France after the German reply was sent. Political figures are doing their best to keep silent about Laval's report. It is now learned that after French Ambassador to the United Kingdom Corbin met with British Foreign Secretary Simon, he telegraphed a report to the French Ministry of Foreign Affairs. It is rumored that the United Kingdom sent a note to the French government, which is probably a false rumor. In fact, the United Kingdom did not send a note. In addition, some newspapers reported that Italy suggested to Britain and France to convene a meeting of the ambassadors of the five countries, Britain, France, Italy, Germany, and Belgium, related to the Air Mutual Assistance Treaty, which is also not true. Generally speaking, the State Council did not make any decision today.

Always Upholding the Agreement

As for the recent exchange of views between Britain and France, it is only about the procedural issues caused by Germany's request to hold individual talks with Britain. In short, the British and French governments fundamentally uphold the London Agreement of February 3. No matter what decision the British government leaders make regarding the demands put forward by Germany, the French authorities express their approval, because of this reason. If the Anglo-German talks that Berlin hopes for can promote the resolution of various outstanding issues, then France will be very happy. Therefore, the goal of the current Anglo-French talks is very limited, that is, to determine how the two governments' reply to Germany should be worded and what the scope should be.

No More Than Two Ways to Reply to Germany

Generally speaking, the reply of Britain and France to Germany will not exceed two ways: either only express acceptance of Germany's request to hold direct talks, and not mention the rest of the issues, and try to raise and discuss them in detail during the direct talks with Germany, or give a true reply to the various basic points of the German letter and reiterate the Anglo-French Agreement of February 3. It is not yet known what kind of decision Britain and France will make, but the ultimate goal currently attempted is to seek peace in Europe under a system in which all countries uniformly obtain security. The goal pursued by British diplomacy is naturally no more than this. (Havas dispatch on the 19th)

Divisive Tricks in Vain

[Paris] According to "Le Petit Parisien," Foreign Minister Laval's report at the State Council yesterday on the progress of the Anglo-French Ministry of Foreign Affairs talks after the German reply was sent clearly expressed satisfaction, saying that the current Anglo-French talks are proceeding smoothly without obstruction. The methods put forward in the German reply not only failed to achieve the purpose of alienating Britain and France, but instead aroused the opposite effect. Britain seems to have the same view as France, believing that the issue of the Air Mutual Assistance Treaty should not be separated from other issues in the London Declaration (referring to Germany's return to the League of Nations, general disarmament treaty, Eastern European mutual assistance treaty, and Danube River treaty, which were not mentioned in the German reply). As for the procedural issues of future negotiations, France will entrust Britain to freely adopt decisions. However, "L'Écho de Paris" said that Germany has violated important international treaties, which is something we should not forget. If Britain changes its original opinion, then France will no longer be able to listen to Britain's representation of France to take responsibility for negotiations with Germany.

Britain Notifies the Soviet Union

According to "L'Intransigeant," since the Anglo-French London talks, Germany has repeatedly attacked the Soviet Union, and Britain has notified the Soviet government of the results of the exchange of views between Britain and France, and said that Britain and France take a consistent attitude on all issues. This kind of notification from Britain to Russia may be regarded by Germany as clear evidence that Britain approves of the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Treaty in spirit. (Havas dispatch on the 22nd)

Russian Ambassador to the UK Declares that Security in Both Eastern and Western Europe Should Be Taken Into Account

[London] Russian Ambassador to the UK Maisky recently issued a declaration, stating the Soviet Union's views on the London Declaration of February 3, which has attracted considerable attention. Maisky's declaration said, "If there is no security and peace in Eastern Europe, then security and peace in Western Europe cannot exist. All parts of the European continent should obtain security at the same time. This section has been stated very clearly in the Anglo-French declaration. In the current mutually involved European situation, if someone advocates first seeking security in Western Europe and disregards security in Eastern Europe, then that person is either ignorant or harbors malicious intentions. It is appropriate for Eastern European countries to be alarmed by this. As for the Air Mutual Assistance Treaty, its purpose is to resist sudden attacks in Western Europe. It is purely a regional mutual assistance treaty with the same basis as the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Treaty. It is a good tool for preventing invasion, but it must be established at the same time as the Eastern European treaty in order to guarantee the peace of the entire Europe. In short, the security and peace of Europe, whether it succeeds or fails, will depend on the success or failure of the Eastern European treaty." (Havas dispatch on the 19th)

British Cabinet Member Sent to Berlin, German Political Circles Eagerly Await

[Berlin] The German government is eagerly looking forward to a British cabinet member coming to Berlin to talk directly with the German government to discuss the various points suggested in the London Declaration. German political figures hope that Britain will send someone to Germany, as this move is really related to Germany's prestige. German newspapers are now making this kind of argument. "Berliner Tageblatt" said, "Hitler is in charge of Germany's major policies. If a British representative comes to Germany to negotiate with Hitler, then he will be able to understand the situation of the new Germany more." "Deutsche Allgemeine Zeitung" said, "Foreign negotiators must now meet with Hitler face-to-face, because the stage of exchanging diplomatic notes has now passed. Since the relationship between the various issues is so important, it is really necessary for the main figures of the various countries to meet once." (Havas dispatch on the 19th)

After the US Gold Clause Case Judgment

The Government Will Ask Congress to Legislate to Eliminate Disputes

Obstacles to Monetary Policy Removed, Silver Faction Active

[New York] The US Treasury Department expressed its opinion that since the cash clause case has ended, the government will proceed with its financial procedures in mid-March, and issue new bonds to replace the bonds that are about to expire. Attorney General Cummings stated today that a legislative act to protect the government based on the gold clause case ruling is not extremely important, but can be regarded as a move to end this dispute. In the future, the opportunity to sue the government no longer exists, but after studying the situation, establishing a kind of law to eliminate all kinds of disputes forever is also a good thing. (Reuters dispatch on the 19th)

[Washington] Attorney General Cummings announced today that the government may ask Congress to pass a bill as soon as possible to consolidate the victory the government won after the Supreme Court declared the gold bond case. After consulting with President Roosevelt at the White House, Cummings said that the purpose of this bill is to prevent continued lawsuits against the government in American courts. The case is still under discussion. Holders of Liberty Bonds have declared that they have suffered heavy losses after the dollar was devalued. The purpose of the case is to prevent these people from suing the government in court. Some legal scholars have stated that the Supreme Court's ruling has not closed the door to this litigation. Observers with vision stated today that the Supreme Court's ruling determines two paths. Future governments must choose one of them. The two paths are (1) all gold should continue to be stored in the treasury, so that the policy of large-scale devaluation of paper money can be sustained, and (2) allow gold to circulate in the market, so that the dollar can restore its previous gold price. However, government spokespersons feel that the obstacles to the progress of monetary policy have now been removed. The New Deal faction is now planning to raise prices and stabilize the value of the US dollar at home and abroad. In the past, it was rumored that an international monetary conference would be convened, but today it was learned that the Supreme Court's ruling has removed the obstacles for the United States to participate in the conference. It is said that the Treasury Department's current plan aims to fix the current dollar value. The government is prepared to curb the abnormal development after the gold bond case was declared, so as to avoid repeating the unpleasant incidents that occurred between June and July 1933. It is learned that the 1933 gold case stipulated that the devaluation limit was 50%. This Supreme Court ruling recognizes that President Roosevelt can manipulate the dollar within this limit. The dollar has now been devalued to 59 cents, so once currency becomes a serious issue for international discussion, there are still 9 cents left for negotiation with foreign countries. Well-informed sources claim that Treasury Department officials are now planning the future steps in the government's currency plan, and raising prices and restoring credit are their current goals. At the same time, the Securities Exchange Commission is still closely monitoring the securities trading market, and is prepared to suspend trading if the market price fluctuates too much. (National Telegram on the 19th)

[New York] James, a professor at the University of Pennsylvania, said that the gold clause issue may still have future developments. Yesterday's Supreme Court ruling cannot prevent foreign governments holding US government bonds from demanding that the US$100 bonds with gold clauses be paid with the current low-value currency of US$169. Private bondholders will also inevitably take this opportunity to transfer all their bonds to foreign governments. However, people in Washington believe that even if foreigners holding bonds ask their government to make this request, it will be invalid, because the bonds are purely domestic debts and are not within the scope of international law. (Reuters dispatch on the 19th)

[Washington] Legal experts in Washington predicted today that the Supreme Court's gold clause ruling may allow American citizens residing in other countries who hold government bonds to sue the government, demanding compensation for losses, because overseas Americans may be able to provide evidence that they have indeed suffered losses due to the devaluation of the dollar and the abolition of gold clause payments. These people purchased bonds before the dollar was devalued, and now they have moved abroad, and the purchasing power of the dollar has been greatly reduced, and the losses are naturally not small. However, the number of such people is very small. Treasury Department officials expressed indifference today. As for foreigners who purchase US bonds, they are not allowed to demand compensation, because the US government issued bonds for the purpose of having the American people buy them. Foreigners who invest are naturally treated equally, and they can never demand compensation because the exchange rate between the dollar and their national currency has changed. (National Telegram on the 19th)

[Paris] France has officially decided not to demand that the United States pay cash in accordance with the original terms of the bonds. All leading banks, such as the Bank of France, have been ordered to reject requests for compensation from people holding US bonds. (National Telegram on the 20th)

US Inflation Faction's Movement to Recoin Silver

Thomas Presents Three Proposals

[Washington] The Senate inflation faction has now begun a new movement advocating the use of silver coins. The Supreme Court's ruling on the gold clause case has, in effect, upheld Congress's right to regulate the national currency. Senator Thomas immediately seized this opportunity and today proposed an amendment to the public works bill, with two objectives: (1) to issue new silver coins to reduce the value of the US dollar; (2) to raise the price of silver to the statutory price of $1.29 per ounce, after which silver coins can be minted without restriction. To achieve this goal, the inflation faction proposes three main methods: A. Issue silver certificates based on $1.29, backed by the Treasury's silver reserves; B. Rapidly implement the Treasury's silver repurchase program; C. International debts should be allowed to be settled in silver. Senator Thomas claims that the issuance of new coins will not exceed $100 million, but it can depress the US dollar to its 1926 value and raise the price of silver, after which the United States can submit an international agreement on a bimetallic system. Whether this amendment will pass is uncertain, but some believe that the gold clause ruling has indeed opened the door for the inflation faction to actively campaign. However, some also express the opinion that the Supreme Court's ruling should curb the trend of inflation, because if the value of the US dollar is repeatedly reduced, holders of gold bonds can sue the government to demand compensation for their losses. The reason why the court denied bondholders the right to claim compensation is that the bondholders have not suffered any damage. Therefore, if there is real damage, the right to claim compensation should certainly not be denied. The New York financial community is quite pleased that the state of uncertainty has now disappeared, and expects that activity in the capital market will soon recover. Although it is not yet known when the International Monetary Conference will be held, one of the major obstacles to international monetary stability has now disappeared. (Reuters, 19th)

[Vienna] Prime Minister Schuschnigg and Foreign Minister Weidgr departed for Paris tonight, accompanied by three officials from the Federal Chancellery and the Ministry of Finance. The Federal Post stated that negotiations are underway regarding Central European issues, and the Prime Minister's trip is timely to complete these negotiations. Japanese Foreign Ministry Council Holds Second Meeting

Discussing Adjustment of Sino-Japanese Trade

[Tokyo] The second meeting of the Foreign Ministry Council was held yesterday at the Foreign Minister's residence. Foreign Minister Hirota, Vice-Minister Shigemitsu, heads of various departments, and ambassadors Ouchida, Nagai, Matsushima, Hayashi, Ota, Nagaoka, Mori, Kasama, Kawashima, and Commercial Counselor Yokotake, Secretary Sudo attended. After Commercial Counselor Yokotake and Secretary Sudo reported on the market situation in China and Central and South America, the following two items were discussed: (1) Concrete measures for economic cooperation following the improvement of Sino-Japanese diplomatic relations, and the readjustment of the recent sharp decline in Sino-Japanese trade; (2) Concrete measures for the economic development of new markets in Central and South America. The meeting adjourned at 10 p.m. Based on the suggestions of Ambassador Kawashima, the following consensus was reached: (1) For countries that were old markets but have adopted trade restriction policies, such as China, France, the United States, Canada, South Africa, and the Soviet Union, efforts should be made to actively ease import restrictions; (2) For countries that were old markets but have not adopted trade restriction policies, such as "Manchukuo," the United Kingdom, the Netherlands, the Straits Settlements, and new markets in Central and South America, such as Central and South America, Turkey, Greece, and Africa, Japan should grant them preferential trade treatment and seek to increase purchases. (Dentsu, 20th)

Italy Restricts Imports of 1,500 Types of Goods

Special Permits Required

[Rome] Today, the Italian government issued a new order listing 1,500 types of goods that require special permits to be imported into Italy. The purpose of this order is partly to restrict Italy's import industry and partly to use it as a bargaining chip to gain preferential treatment for Italian exports abroad. The restrictions range from 35% to 100% and will take effect on March 31. Coal, machinery, woolen sweaters, leather goods, steel, fish, cotton for manufacturing, linen, hemp, tobacco, alcohol, tea, and biscuits are all among the goods that require special permits to be imported. (Reuters, 19th)

UK Revenue and Expenditure Statistics

[London] The Treasury Department issued statistics tonight showing that national tax revenue for the fiscal year to February 16 totaled £593,878,820, compared to £609,701,084 for the same period last year. The budget estimate was £706,000,000, leaving six weeks to complete the fiscal year, and requiring revenue of £112,000,000 to reach the budget target. Expenditure for the same period was £622,000,000, compared to £608,000,000 last year. The budget figure was £711,000,000. Income tax revenue for the past week was £14,000,000, bringing the total to £175,669,000 by February 16, compared to £173,594,000 for the same period last year. (Reuters, 19th)

UK House of Commons Studies Indian Constitutional Amendment Bill

[London] The House of Commons began studying the India Bill today. The first important issue it dealt with was the appointment of the Viceroy of India. Labour MP Thorne moved a motion to establish a permanent committee composed of former Viceroys of India, with whom the Prime Minister must first consult before appointing a Viceroy under the new constitution. Thorne believed that the Viceroy was the cornerstone of the entire constitutional structure, and the selection of a person for this important position should not be influenced by party politics. Indian Affairs Secretary Hoare stated that the purpose of this motion was to ensure that the selection of the Viceroy was not dominated by partisan politics, and he expressed sympathy, but he could not agree to transferring the responsibility of the Prime Minister and the Cabinet to a committee. The Liberal Party and the Labour Party also opposed this motion, so the motion was eventually withdrawn. Conservative MP Hulbert proposed an amendment stipulating in the constitution that the Viceroy could not be removed from office except by a petition from both houses of Parliament to the King, but this proposal was defeated by 324 votes to 49. The issue of the All-India Federation was then discussed, and Hulbert proposed the establishment of a Grand Indian Advisory Council, composed of representatives from the Indian princely states and British India. (Reuters, 20th)

Another German Espionage Case

[Berlin] It is reported that two more male spies have recently been tried by the regular court for seeking secrets of naval affairs. Unless pardoned by Führer Hitler, they will be sentenced to death. However, the details have not been announced by the authorities. (Reuters, 20th)

Number of Japanese Opium Addicts in Manchuria on the Rise

The Tokyo Hochi Shimbun reported on the 15th that the history of Japanese in Manchuria is more than 30 years old. Since the September 18th Incident, the number of people moving in has been increasing day by day. Unexpectedly, the number of people who smoke opium and use morphine has also been increasing. Among them, young people in their prime are the most numerous. The reason for this is that Japanese people in border areas lack any kind of comfort, so once they set foot in the red-light district, they are all moved by curiosity and swallow opium. After that, they gradually become addicted and it is difficult to break the habit. In the future, as negotiations with Manchuria become more complex, the number of Japanese opium addicts will inevitably increase.

New York Commodity Market Prices

Luan County Local Troops Suddenly Clash

Both Sides Suffer Casualties

Neighboring Counties Under Martial Law

Beiping News Luan County War Zone Security First Brigade, led by Liu Zuozhou, recently reorganized the county's militia, sending many trainers to various districts, resulting in dissatisfaction from the militia. Gao Congshan, the head of the Third District Militia, and Yin Laosan, among others, secretly gathered 4,000 militiamen and went to Duoyutun and Machengle Camp to disarm the militia trainers sent by Liu, and tied up the school principals and civil servants appointed by Liu, and transported them in 20 carts to outside the north gate of Bencheng, and planned to confiscate the firearms of the Bencheng militia. At this time, Liu had received the report and urgently sent more than 1,000 cavalrymen to go, resulting in a conflict with the militia in Bencheng. The battle lasted for about three hours, and the cavalrymen were defeated and retreated. Liu continued to send more than 2,000 men to go, and the militia retreated. It is estimated that two cavalrymen were killed, one militiaman was killed, and more than 100 were injured. Luan County Magistrate Chen Cengshi, after the incident, telegraphed to the provincial government and the special commissioner's office to consult on mediation. The special commissioner's office also sent personnel to go, joining local gentry to run around, but both sides wanted to try their strength, resulting in no clue. Tao Shangming had decided to return to Tangshan with Zhao Lei on the 19th to mediate, but the local troops had contact again at 8:00 PM on the 18th, and it did not stop until the morning of the 19th. Both sides of the local troops had casualties, and the fighting in the Bencheng area was fierce, and the situation was extremely bad. Tangshan, Fengrun, Qian'an, and Zunhua, neighboring counties, have all been placed under martial law since the 18th. The local militias of these counties have also been transferred to the border area to strengthen prevention.

Zhao Lei, the commander of the First Battalion of the Luan-Yu District Security Team, was summoned by the War Zone Clearing Committee yesterday to come to Beiping to meet with the standing committee members Zhu Shiqin and Yin Rugeng to discuss the troop rotation matters of the War Zone Security Team. It was decided that Feng Shoupeng's unit of the Yutian Security Supplementary Corps, all 1,000 men, would be transferred to Tongxian and Kaiping, with 500 men stationed in each place. Zhao himself, due to the conflict between the local troops in Luan County, is scheduled to leave Beiping and return to Tangshan on the morning of the 20th (19th).

Hebei Provincial Government Decides to Move to Baoding

The Provincial Government Dispatches Personnel to Survey Housing

The Department of Civil Affairs to be Reorganized on March 1st

Tianjin Dispatch: Regarding the issue of the Hebei Provincial Government moving to Baoding, Chairman Yu (Xuezhong) dispatched Jiang Chunyan, the Deputy Adjutant of the 51st Army, ten days ago to Baoding to investigate available housing. Jiang returned during the Spring Festival and reported that although the old Governor's Office buildings were dilapidated, they could still be used after repairs. However, they were not as spacious as the Tianjin Provincial Government buildings, and it would not be possible to combine the military headquarters into one office. It would be necessary to consult with the Baoding Headquarters and move to another location, letting the old Imperial Palace buildings be used for the military headquarters, which would be sufficient. After receiving the report, the province will send workers this month to repair the buildings before moving. Although the regulations for joint office work have long been drafted, they have not been implemented immediately because the move to Baoding is imminent. Instead of making a troublesome merger now, it is better to do it all at once in the future. Before the move to Baoding is implemented, the Department of Civil Affairs, in order to reduce expenses and increase administrative efficiency, has decided to reorganize on March 1st. The subordinate Provincial General Affairs Office, the Autonomous Planning Office, the Rural Pacification Office, and the Relief Association will all be abolished and incorporated into the Department. The tasks to be handled by each committee will be re-divided, and a new section will be added, making a total of five sections along with the original four, each responsible for its own duties. Secretaries, inspectors, and technical staff will be placed directly under the control of the Director. In the past, the Department of Civil Affairs' annual budget was 186,384 yuan, with a monthly expenditure of 15,532 yuan. Later, due to financial difficulties, the budget was repeatedly cut, and in the 22nd year of the Republic, the actual monthly expenditure was only 6,200 yuan. The monthly expenditure for the Department's inspectors was initially 2,160 yuan, but was recently reduced to 1,824 yuan. The Department's workload has increased year by year. Initially, the annual number of issued documents was over 80,000, but last year it increased to over 170,000. The personnel of the Police Department, the Rural Pacification Office, and the Autonomous Planning Office are all concurrently serving from within the Department, and their duties are very heavy. This time, the Department has decided to reorganize, and the staff's treatment will also be slightly improved, and the progress of work can be accelerated compared to before. The duties of each of the five sections have been approved by the provincial government's regular meeting. The first section is responsible for the appointment, dismissal, promotion, transfer, assessment, and reward of county magistrates, and the organization and rectification of county governments. The second section is responsible for planning autonomy, land surveying, household registration statistics, and elections. The third section is responsible for water and land public safety, guarding rural areas, suppressing bandits, and county defense and foreign affairs. The fourth section is responsible for grain storage and disaster relief, as well as other social relief, opium prohibition, drug prohibition, sanitation, epidemic prevention, social customs, religion, and preservation of antiquities. The fifth section is responsible for guarding seals, storing, receiving, dispatching, copying, and proofreading documents, and accounting and general affairs. In addition, there are positions such as secretary's office, technical officer, technician, inspector, and secretary, but their authority has not been increased, only reorganized compared to before. (17th)

Central Government Sends Engineering Experts to Survey the Confucius Temple in Qufu

Shandong Provincial Government Sends Personnel to Join the Survey

Personnel Investigating Descendants of the Four Sages Depart in the Same Car

Jinan Dispatch: Tang Wencong and Zhong Lingji, section chiefs dispatched by the Ministries of Interior and Education, and Liang Encheng (eldest son of Liang Qichao), a specially appointed ancient architectural engineering expert from the central government, recently contacted Zhang Honglie, Director of the Construction Department, and He Siyuan, Director of the Education Department, regarding the matter of repairing the Confucius Temple. The Construction Department dispatched technicians Wang Jizhong and Yang Judou (who had estimated the Confucius Temple project twice), and Xiaoqing River engineer Yu Gaomin, who were scheduled to depart from Jinan at 9:00 am on the 19th to accompany Liang et al. to Qufu to jointly survey the Confucius Temple. Kong Lingcan, the secretary of the Education Department, went to Qufu on the night of the 18th to prepare to welcome them and lead the survey on behalf of the Kong clan. It is said that after the survey is completed, Liang, Tang, and Zhong will return to Beijing or Jinan, because this matter is of great importance and cannot be designed and estimated without several surveys. On the morning of the 18th, the provincial government hosted a banquet for Liang and his party. During the banquet, Liang talked about the steps of the project, believing that the first survey would only be a general one, looking at the extent of the damage. The second survey would be more detailed, and high scaffolding must be erected to see the details from a high place. The third step is to design. The steps of the project should first repair the framework, and then decorate the exterior, with equal emphasis on firmness and not losing the original appearance. It was previously estimated that 1 million yuan was needed. Although he has not yet personally surveyed, he roughly said that it may not cost 1 million yuan. The future project will probably have to be done by themselves. It is expected that no one will dare to contract for the work, because when Zhang Zongchang was in Shandong, he repaired the Xiangdian once, contracted for 60,000 yuan, and ended up spending 80,000 yuan, and the contractor even lost 7,000 yuan. Therefore, no one may dare to contract for the repair of the Confucius Temple this time. It is also said that the central government's method of apportioning funds to the provinces for the repair of the Confucius Temple is that, except for remote and poor provinces, the inland provinces will be apportioned a maximum of 260,000 yuan and a minimum of 60,000 yuan. After the banquet, Liang and his party went to the Provincial Library to visit and toured Daming Lake. They went to Qufu on the morning of the 19th. In addition to organizing the Confucius Temple, the central government is also investigating the descendants of the Four Sages, Yan, Zeng, Si, and Meng, and will grant each of them the title of Sacrificial Officer to honor the sacrifices, and will also provide assistance to the descendants of the Sages to study. The two departments of education and civil affairs of this province were ordered to investigate and report the descendants of the Sages. Now, the Education Department has sent Inspector Xu Meisheng, and the Civil Affairs Department has sent Inspector Li Weixia, who are scheduled to go south in the same car with the experts surveying the Confucius Temple on the morning of the 19th. According to Kong Lingcan, the uncle of Kong Decheng, each of the descendants of the Sages has a genealogy to check, which should not be very difficult. As far as he knows, only the Zeng clan (in Jiaxiang County) is slightly sparse in population. The current Zeng Sacrificial Officer, Zeng Fansan, is still young and is involved in a lawsuit. During the Southern Song Dynasty, a part of the descendants of Zeng migrated south with the Song Dynasty, so there is a branch of the Zeng clan in Zhejiang now. The current president of the Shandong Agricultural College, Zeng Shengzhi, is their descendant. As for the Kong clan, there are a total of 60 branches. They are currently revising the genealogy. When the Song Dynasty moved south, the eldest branch also went south with them, which is the Southern Branch. Now, the clan in Quzhou, Zhejiang, has the largest population. Perhaps the Southern Branch was not allowed to come north, so they gave the responsibility of sacrifice to the second branch, which is the one in Qufu now. In addition, there is a branch in Shanxi, of which Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi is a member. He is a member of the Yan character generation of the Ming Dynasty and emigrated to Shanxi to do business. (18th)

Jiangxi Province Reorganizes Administrative Regions

— Boundaries of Each County Will be Redrawn —

Nanchang Dispatch: Jiangxi Province is surrounded by mountains on all sides, and the administrative regions of each county have always been uneven, which causes many inconveniences in administrative facilities and local management. This is especially true in southern Jiangxi and the remote border areas. For example, Ningdu County is too large in area, and the four townships are beyond reach. Chongyi County is located in the remote northeast border, and Xingguo County is located in the southwest, with each township too far from the county government. Also, the Longgang, Tengtian, Cihua, Zhaoqiao, Fenggang, and Dawen areas, which were established separately during the bandit suppression period, are all adjacent to two provinces or four or five counties, forming a "three-no-care" situation. The provincial government believes that the administrative region is of great importance to administrative efficiency, and especially for handling rural pacification, searching for scattered bandits, organizing Baojia, and building roads, it will not be successful without reorganizing the regions. It has decided to actively proceed in accordance with the Outline for Reorganizing Administrative Regions and the Regulations on Surveying Boundaries of Provinces, Cities, and Counties promulgated by the Ministry of Interior, starting with the newly recovered areas in southern Jiangxi. The provincial government has ordered the personnel sent to Ningdu, Huichang, Anyuan, Xunwu, and Xingguo to work with local officials to investigate and survey the boundaries of each region, draw maps, and report in detail, so that after review, they can be reorganized and redrawn, or new governments can be established, so that they are convenient in terms of natural form, county jurisdiction, and administrative facilities, so as to avoid providing opportunities for bandits to mix in again and to stabilize the local area. (27th)

Jiangnan Defense Army Breaks Bandit Nest in Youshan

Small Gangs of Zhan and Yang are Gradually Eliminated

Guangzhou Dispatch: After the large gang of Communist bandits in southern Jiangxi fled west into Sichuan, only the remaining bandits of Ye Jianying's gang, six or seven thousand, are scattered between Yudu and Xingguo. A few days ago, they attacked Niuling from Xiaoxi, trying to capture Xinfeng and plunder food. They were severely attacked by the Xinfeng defense army, and the bandit crowd fled to Maling. The Guangdong army has now sent teams to encircle and suppress them, and at the same time, they are searching for bandit traces in Xiaoxi. Yesterday, the First Army also learned from scouts that there was still a gang of Communist bandits hiding in Youshan, on the border of Guangdong and Jiangxi. The ridge connects the counties of Dayu, Nanxiong, Xinfeng, and Shixing for hundreds of miles, with deep mountains, dense forests, and narrow paths. It is not easy to go deep into the mountains to search for them without a large army. The bandit gang in the mountain is led by bandits Yang Bensheng and Zhan Biao, each with about eight or nine hundred people. When the Communist bandits tried to capture Xinfeng a few days ago, the two small gangs hid in the mountain, waiting for opportunities to steal and attack. Therefore, the transportation on the border of Guangdong and Jiangxi has often been destroyed by the gang. The defense army believes that this is a hidden danger and sent troops to search and suppress them the day before yesterday. After receiving the order, Regiment Commander Liao led his troops through Lidong, Dengfang, and Zhongzhan to the Xinxiong border area, encountering more than a dozen small gangs of scattered bandits along the way. They finally broke the bandit nest in Youshan, burned down more than a dozen bandit strongholds, and captured three or four hundred local Communists alive. Every time Regiment Commander Liao recovers a place, he divides a company to garrison and prevent the bandits from regrouping. On the one hand, he sends teams to surround the remaining bandits, and now there are only about five or six hundred remaining bandits, with less than two hundred guns, which is not a cause for concern. For the sake of organizing the bandit area, the defense army has recently recruited local people to return to their hometowns, restore farming, and build roads to facilitate transportation, and has also established civilian primary schools to influence poor children and prevent them from being misled by Communist heresies and becoming bandits. (13th)

Jiangsu Department of Finance Reorganizes Procedures for Collecting Land Tax in Various Counties

Eight Principles for Reorganization and Rectification are Established

Zhenjiang Dispatch: The Jiangsu Department of Finance has repeatedly ordered the improvement of land tax collection procedures in various counties. The county governments have followed and implemented the orders, and there are many who are brave in reform, but there are also those who cling to old habits and are perfunctory. In particular, the preparatory procedures for starting collection in various counties are extremely cumbersome, and they are often carried out in their own way due to old habits, allowing clerks to engage in malpractices and not following the regulations, resulting in chaotic and varied procedures for collecting grain in various counties, making it difficult to investigate and verify. The government finds it difficult to audit, and the work of collecting tax has almost become a specialized secret affair, which cannot be handled without those clerks. Now, in order to unify and reorganize the procedures for collecting the first installment of land tax in the 24th year of the Republic in various counties, the Department of Finance has specially established eight principles for reorganization, and ordered them to be promulgated to various counties on the 19th (except for the seven counties of Zhenjiang, Yixing, Kunshan, Jiading, Liyang, Jiangyin, and Baoshan, which are included in the pilot program for improving the land tax collection system) to follow and implement, so as to completely eliminate the bad habits of slackness from the first installment of land tax in the 24th year of the Republic. The eight principles are as follows:

Principles of Reorganization (1) From the 24th year of the Republic, all counties shall implement the principle of combining busy and transport taxes, and dividing the collection into two installments, four-six. Those counties that have not yet implemented this principle shall calculate and prepare the forms two months before the start of the first installment of the 24th year, and report them to this department for approval. If anyone still follows old habits and requests changes after the fact, it will not be allowed. (2) Two months before the start of the first installment of land tax in the 24th year, each county shall prepare a collection register with the full names, plot numbers, Mu allocation, or silver-rice amounts (the principle is that the Mu allocation and silver-rice amounts are both available, and if there is no Mu allocation, the silver-rice amount should be noted) of all grain households in the county, and the amount of tax to be collected (referring to the total amount of regular and surtax, Mu donation, collection fee, etc., not just the amount of regular tax to be collected converted into silver and rice). It must be filled in according to the regulations in detail, and must not be perfunctory or omitted. Serial tickets shall be prepared based on the collection register. The form of the collection register and serial ticket is attached to each county for reference. (3) When preparing the serial tickets, each county shall pay attention to the following matters: A. The serial ticket should be divided into three copies: stub, license, and notice, all of which should indicate the name of the grain household, the plot number, the Mu allocation, the amount of grain, and the date. B. The serial ticket should be prepared in two installments in principle. If any county has special circumstances, it may apply to prepare them together in two installments, but the license copy of the second installment must be kept blank, and then filled in and stamped after the autumn survey is finalized and the deduction is verified. C. All serial tickets must be filled in with regular script. The grain amount column must be stamped with a lead-type wooden stamp, and must not be written in demon characters or other simplified characters. D. The amount of grain to be paid as stated on the serial ticket shall include all provincial and county surtaxes, donations, collection fees, handling fees, and writing fees (the Mu donations of previous land surveys were added by stamping or collecting receipts separately, but from the first installment of the 24th year, they should be abolished and uniformly calculated into various Mu donations). The total grain amount must be consistent with the cash paid by the owner, otherwise, they are specially allowed to report to the provincial department for investigation and handling according to law. (4) From the 24th year, all procedures for preparing registers and serial tickets shall be completed before the start of each installment. They must not be deliberately delayed, or even submit a blank document after the start of collection. In the future, they must report to the department for approval in advance before collection can begin. (5) Before the start of each installment of land tax, each county must first distribute the serial ticket notice to each owner in advance for inspection, and post the land grade, tax rate, tax amount, and other matters that the owner should pay attention to, and print a brief explanation book and distribute it to the village and town Baojia leaders for dissemination and publicity, so as to encourage the owners to pay in large numbers and eliminate the bad habit of clerks collecting and paying on their behalf. (6) Before the start of the first installment of land tax in each year, each county must list in detail the tax rate per Mu, the total amount of provincial and county regular and surtaxes to be collected, and their percentage ratios, and report them to the Department of Finance for approval. The form is attached later. (7) At least the following kinds of land tax collection books and registers must be prepared in each county: A. For audit purposes, a serial ticket registration book (i.e., daily receipt book, flow book, or circular hall book) and a serial ticket report form shall be prepared. B. For tax collection purposes, a cash daily receipt book, a payment book, and a daily report of tax collected shall be prepared. The forms of the aforementioned books and registers shall be determined and issued by the department for use. If there are special circumstances and other books and registers need to be added, the facts must be reported in detail and the form of the books and registers must be submitted together to the department for approval before they can be printed and prepared for use, so as to achieve uniformity. (8) In the past, land tax in various counties was collected by setting up counters according to old practices. The organization of the grain counters shall be strictly reorganized by the county from the 24th year. Except for the serial number management room, which shall be inspected and managed by personnel sent by the county, the rest shall be based on the principle of establishing three separate parts: calculation, collection, and issuance of serial numbers. It is best if the collection part can be collected by the treasury, otherwise, it should be carefully entrusted by the county to prevent overcharges. The total number of daily receipts and serial numbers issued should be consistent, and the accounting director sent by the department should be responsible for spot checks and audits at any time. (20th)
