Gu Xin-yi Issues Important Statement on Foreign Rice

The Quantity of Foreign Rice Imports Should Be Determined by Needs

Supply and Demand Being Equivalent, Ordering Should Be Restricted Hereafter

Foreign Trade in Coarse Grains Has Turned into a Surplus

According to the Da Gong News Agency, Gu Xin-yi, chairman of the Municipal Coarse Grains Trade Association, gave an important statement yesterday to the Da Gong News Agency reporter who visited him regarding the process of ordering foreign rice, which is recorded as follows:

Comparison of Foreign Rice Imports Over the Years

China is an agricultural country, and grain can originally be self-sufficient. However, due to backward domestic production, frequent disasters, and the surplus of foreign agricultural products, which are actively dumped, the import of foreign rice has formed a major social problem today. Tracing back to 1929, the Jiang-Zhe region suffered a drought, and there was panic over food. It was necessary to rely on a huge amount of foreign rice. Therefore, in 1930, imports reached more than 8 million bags, which was truly an unprecedented record. However, it was also fortunate to have this huge supply of foreign rice that the rice price could be maintained at a maximum of 23 or 24 yuan per picul. In 1931, there were floods in the Yangtze River basin, but according to national harvest statistics, the shortage of rice was still limited. Therefore, in 1932, there were not many foreign rice imports. More than 500,000 bags imported by a certain foreign firm at that time were not needed in reality, and more than 300,000 bags were left in stock. From 1932, there were consecutive years of good harvests, and domestic rice was abundant, and prices plummeted. In 1933, in Shanghai alone, not only was not a single grain of foreign rice imported, but even the rice left in stock by a certain foreign firm was still ignored. It was not until last year, when the drought developed, that it was sold off at a low price. Thus, it can be seen that the need for foreign rice and the quantity of its import are all determined by the lack or abundance of domestic grain.

Last Year's Orders Matched Supply and Demand

Last year, there was a severe drought, and the degree of famine and panic over food throughout the country was almost the same as in 1930. Therefore, there was an urgent need for foreign rice, and the import of foreign rice was continuous. In order to ensure the appropriateness of supply and demand, the association should conduct a thorough investigation. According to recent investigation reports from various foreign firms, as of January 18 this year, the total number of orders reached more than 6.3 million bags. In addition to the previous sales of more than 1.8 million bags, the current number of bags being shipped but not yet arrived and those that have been ordered but not yet shipped totals about 4 million bags (of which about 500,000 bags will arrive in Shanghai around February 15). Combined with the recent sales of about 500,000 bags, the total is about 4.5 million bags. This is the general situation obtained by the association's investigation before January 18, which is also consistent with the total number of foreign rice registrations by the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs, and should not be far from the truth. Furthermore, according to the sales estimates of foreign rice, the average daily sales of various provinces is 20,000 bags, and the local sales in Shanghai is 5,000 bags, totaling 6 months until mid-August of the lunar calendar, and the total sales volume is exactly 4.5 million bags, which is consistent with the total number of orders obtained in the previous investigation, and the supply and demand are exactly equivalent. Therefore, the association believes that it is necessary to stop ordering from now on, and has tried to repeatedly warn the industry, and is even preparing to submit it to the authorities for a fundamental ban.

Foreign Trade in Coarse Grains Has Turned into a Surplus

As for the relationship between foreign rice imports and the money supply, of the one million bags of foreign rice currently stored in Shanghai, about half have not yet paid for the documents, plus the 3.5 million bags that have not yet been shipped, totaling 4 million bags. The average market price per bag is 11 yuan and 56 cents. Excluding the import tax of 3 yuan and 56 cents, which is government revenue, each bag is worth about 8 yuan, so the total value is 32 million yuan. The number of excess imports of foreign goods is increasing day by day, which is already alarming, and adding the ordering of foreign rice and the outflow of such a large amount of money, it is difficult to avoid the serious attention of the social community. However, in reality, the coarse grains industry has been engaged in foreign trade. In 1934, Shanghai and Hankou exported sesame seeds worth about 15 million yuan, Qingdao exported peanut kernels and peanut oil worth about 13 million yuan, and other oil cakes and beans exported worth about 8 million yuan, totaling about 36 million yuan. If only the current imports of the coarse grains industry are calculated, it has already turned into a surplus. If domestic agricultural products have a bumper harvest and foreign rice is no longer needed and not imported, then the surplus of coarse grains will be even more considerable.

Terminating Orders Poses No Threat of Surplus

Moreover, when rice prices plummeted in 1933, the association was the first to appeal to the government to increase the import tax on foreign rice in order to enrich the national treasury and to achieve the practical effect of rescuing rural areas. Today, the situation has changed, and domestic rice is lacking. The industry is entrusted by mainland customers to order foreign rice to provide assistance, which is something that has to be done. Without this assistance, the current rise in rice prices would have already surpassed the rice prices of 1930, and the social situation would not be as peaceful as it is today. Moreover, rescuing the people's food supply cannot be compared with the import of other foreign luxury goods. In summary, according to the above, the current situation of foreign rice purchasing and sales is such that supply and demand are exactly equivalent. Terminating orders from now on poses no threat of surplus. If orders continue to be placed without limit, it will inevitably lead to an oversupply. Then, the precedent of a certain foreign firm's stock of foreign rice being ignored is a lesson that is not far away. It is hoped that grain merchants will be vigilant together.

The Central News Agency reporter obtained a letter from Wu Tiecheng to the people of the Philippine Islands (translated from the original English manuscript) and Wang Zhengting's article "The Mission of the Tourist Group," which are recorded separately as follows:

Wu Tiecheng's Letter

In recent years, the economic panic has affected the whole world, and the countries along the Pacific coast have also been affected. If we do not adopt the path of "peace and amity," we will not be able to solve the economic crisis and seek prosperity for each other. The political leaders of the Philippine Islands have always been known to the world for their virtue and patriotism. I firmly believe that they will be able to maintain friendly relations with all countries along this peaceful path. Moreover, the Philippine Islands are a land endowed by nature, and they should be able to use their unique endowment to make great contributions to the welfare of mankind. Our country is a close neighbor, and we wish that the "Pearl of the Pacific" will soon realize its mission, and we hope that the cultural and economic relations between the two peoples will become more developed. I personally express my sympathy for any friendly movement between the two peoples and will do my best to support it in order to enhance the friendly relations between China and the Philippines. For hundreds of years, the Chinese people who have traveled far across the oceans to trade in the Philippine Islands have mostly been successful, but they have never interfered in the internal affairs of the Philippine Islands. Based on this historical fact, I am more confident that the two peoples of China and the Philippines will be able to get along with each other and become more and more friendly.

Wang Zhengting's Article

The Chen Bao has a special issue on the departure of the tourist group to the Philippines and asked me to write an article to briefly explain the meaning of the mission of the tourist group. The diplomatic relations between China and the Philippines have always been known for their cordiality, and the relationship between the two countries has a long history, which is deep and close, and needs no further explanation. I have studied the Chinese who have left their motherland, sailed far away, and worked hard to achieve today's success. Their past achievements have been admired by foreigners. However, since foreigners have taken control of the ruling power in various places, they have always harbored discrimination against our Chinese because of racial and national concepts, which is regrettable. In particular, the leaders of the Philippine Islands have always held good feelings towards our Chinese. Therefore, the Chinese in the Philippines who are rich in ideas and capable of implementing their plans and fully developing their careers, so that the Chinese in the Philippines have a thriving trend, which is gratifying. I have studied that the customs and habits of the Philippine Islands have gradually become Europeanized during the 300 years of Spanish rule. After the Americans came, the Filipinos became more aware of the need to work hard to enlighten their knowledge, exercise their bodies, develop industry and commerce, and improve their political status. Recently, with less than one-third of the national land being cultivated, they are also striving to advance, studying agriculture and forestry, and opening up sports fields in many gaps for competition and competition, so sports are very developed. The Philippines has won the top prize in the past Far Eastern Games. The Filipinos are also hospitable, and the carnivals and Christmas festivals that are popular in Europe and the United States are held with enthusiasm every year. Recently, in politics, they have been able to strive for independence. They are truly worthy of a new world in the old world. Whether in spirit or in material, they will surely shine in the future among the various ethnic groups in Southeast Asia, which is worthy of our reference. In addition to visiting the scenery, the tourist group is willing to conduct a detailed study and thorough understanding of the entire situation in the Philippines in order to provide guidance for the development of various undertakings in our country. At the same time, they will also promote Chinese culture to their country as much as possible in order to promote a deep understanding and understanding of the motherland among the overseas Chinese in Southeast Asia. This is the mission of the tourist group.

The Aviation Association Entrusts Banks, Shops, Etc. to Collect Aviation Donations

According to the Central News Agency, since the second fundraising campaign began, the office of the chief captain of the China Aviation Association has been actively raising donations to gather the strength of the people to assist the government in enriching national defense. The work is very tense. The general manager leads the staff day and night. In order to facilitate the donation of aviation patriotism donations by all sectors of the city, the association has specially entrusted banks, money shops, companies, shops, restaurants, etc. throughout the city to collect donations and has formulated seven measures for collection, which are as follows: 1. The office of the chief captain of the Shanghai fundraising team of the China Aviation Association has specially entrusted banks, money shops, companies, shops, restaurants, etc. throughout the city to collect aviation patriotism donations in order to facilitate the donation of aviation patriotism donations by all sectors of the city. 2. Banks, money shops, companies, shops, restaurants, etc. should hang advertisements and publicity materials for raising aviation patriotism donations on the facade to promote attention from all sectors of the city. 3. Banks, money shops, companies, shops, restaurants, etc. should collect aviation patriotism donations for a period of six months, which may be extended if necessary. 4. Banks, money shops, companies, shops, restaurants, etc. should collect aviation patriotism donations in any amount. After receiving the donations, the first copy of the donation receipt issued by the office should be given to the donor, and the second copy of the receipt should be submitted to the office. At the end of the donation, the third copy of the stub and unused receipts should be sent to the office for verification. 5. Banks, money shops, companies, shops, restaurants, etc. should notify the office of the amount of aviation patriotism donations collected at any time in order to be disclosed in the newspaper. 6. Banks, money shops, companies, shops, restaurants, etc. should make a settlement of the aviation patriotism donations collected every fifteen days and remit the donations collected to the office. 7. If the donation receipts of banks, money shops, companies, shops, restaurants, etc. are not enough, they should be collected from the office on the third floor of the YMCA at Baxianqiao. In addition, the office has specially requested the Central Bank, the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, the Shanghai Bank, and the Bank of Shanghai to collect membership fees and aviation patriotism donations for the convenience of all fundraising teams in paying membership fees and aviation patriotism donations.

If there is insufficient time, energy, or strength, the captains can consider the situation and add deputy captains and team members to take on the work in order to achieve practical results. If the various fundraising documents previously sent are not enough, please notify the office at any time by letter or telegram, and they will be sent immediately. Captains are also requested to report any opinions or contributions to the fundraising campaign at any time in order to communicate information and jointly plan the progress.

The Agricultural Conference of the Bank of China Opened Yesterday

Continued Discussion of Key Points Today and Tomorrow

According to the Central News Agency, in order to revive the rural economy, the Bank of China launched agricultural loans two years ago. Branches in Hebei, Shandong, Henan, Shaanxi, Anhui, and Jiangsu provinces and cities separately dispatched personnel to handle the loans. In the past two years, due to the good social order in the above-mentioned provinces, the business has been able to develop steadily. By the end of last year, the highest record for loans had reached 2 million yuan. Recently, in order to determine rural investment and study the revival of the rural economy, an agricultural conference was specially held, starting yesterday, at the bank's general management office on Sanma Road. More than 20 agricultural personnel from branches in various provinces and cities attended the conference. Yesterday, they reported on the rural loan situation in their respective locations. Today and tomorrow, they will present various opinions or proposals for discussion and research. The conference is expected to last about four days. All records and written reports will be published in the bank's annual report at the end of March and the beginning of April. In order to understand the bank's recent agricultural loan situation, the Central News Agency reporter specially visited the responsible persons of the bank's secretariat and business department yesterday. According to them, the past two years have been experimental in nature, so only 2 million yuan was loaned. There are many investments in agriculture by the banking industry in the northwest provinces, but due to the vast area, there is still room for development. The bank's loans are mostly invested in product warehouses and credit loans. If there are no products, there is no need to loan. However, if you want to develop credit loans, it is very easy, but for the sake of prudence, it has not been expanded. The best results have been achieved in Shaanxi. Since Shao Lizi took office in Shaanxi, he has paid close attention to the suffering of the people, especially the development of water conservancy, which is more closely related to the welfare of farmers, so the agricultural loan results are the best. Shandong Chairman Han Fuqu also pays attention to the livelihood of farmers, so the results are also good. This type of loan is difficult to achieve without government assistance. The future progress will still be based on the nature of the experiment, and then efforts will be made to develop it in order to revive the rural economy of our country.

Page 12

Mr. Struthers, British Cooperative Expert, Discusses Goals of Cooperative Movement

Continuation of Speech at Shanghai Bank Agricultural Cooperation Meeting

According to statistics from the International Statistical Bureau in Geneva, there are currently 500,000 cooperatives worldwide. Since the cooperative movement shifted from urban to rural areas, there have been slight changes. Initially, the founding fathers of cooperation in Britain and France hoped to solve all the world's problems through the cooperative movement. However, after a century of experience, this kind of all-encompassing ideal can be considered a failure. The current trend is for each cooperative to specialize in one type of business, with only one cooperative of the same nature in a locality, but multiple cooperatives with different natures. However, there are many cooperative instructors in China who advocate running several types of businesses, which is a mistake. The experience from around the world proves that cooperatives that engage in many businesses often fail. Currently, there are still some cooperatives in China lacking accurate statistics, approximately over 10,000. According to Mr. Struthers' observation, many of them are difficult to call genuine cooperatives, and it is feared that there will not be much improvement in the future. Given the backwardness of the Chinese people's education and knowledge, it is of course impossible to expect them to manage cooperatives themselves, but it is also impossible to let them rely on others forever. Chinese cooperative instructors should explain the meaning of cooperation to farmers before organizing them and train them. For those already organized, their content should be inspected frequently. There are two things to pay attention to when organizing: (1) Members should be able to understand the purpose and meaning of cooperation; (2) After organization, regardless of the scope, it should be treated as a business. Special instructions should be given to cooperative members in China who already have some knowledge. It is easier for instructors to guide cooperatives with simple businesses; it is much more difficult for others. Currently, credit cooperatives are the most numerous in China, with about 100 marketing cooperatives and 50 utility and supply cooperatives. These numbers may not be entirely accurate. Within these 10,000 cooperatives, there are credit cooperatives that also engage in marketing, as well as other cooperatives that engage in various combinations. It is best for a cooperative to operate one type of business. Training for instructors should focus on two things: one is the training of members, and the other is strict attention to business methods to make them rational. Because the cooperative movement is extremely important to China's development, the government should also pay special attention and assistance. Mr. Struthers studies marketing, while I will talk to you about credit cooperation. There are three purposes for establishing credit cooperatives: (1) to enable members to escape the oppression of debt; (2) to prevent those without debt from being oppressed by debt in the future; (3) to train members to know how to save and become citizens with good virtues. The debts of Chinese farmers are currently not as significant as those in India and Egypt. I fear that in twenty or thirty years, they will increase day by day. You may not believe it, but I would like to say a word: in twenty years, politics will gradually become clear and social order will gradually become stable. This is something that all Chinese people hope for. However, the clearer the politics, the more the people's debts will increase. Let me give some reasons for debt: (1) Borrowers are willing to borrow, and lenders are willing to lend. If lenders are unwilling to lend, then borrowers will have no way to incur debt; (2) There is a need to borrow, and there is a willingness to borrow, and at the same time, there is also debt. If someone is diligent and does not borrow, then they will not incur debt. If someone does not want to borrow money, they will not end up in debt. There are also two reasons for lending money to people: (1) having the ability to lend money; (2) needing to lend money. We can say that usury and exorbitant taxes are phenomena of poverty. We study under what circumstances those with money are willing to lend money, that is, when politics is clear, transportation is convenient, and laws are effective, lenders can easily sue debtors and confiscate and manage their land and property without suffering losses. Therefore, when there is legal protection, those with money are willing to lend money. At this time, Chinese politics is inferior to India's, so the oppression of farmers' debt is not very heavy. This does not mean that good politics is useless, but only that while politics is clear, it is also necessary to prevent the increase of people's debt. A hundred years ago, the people of India, except for a few cities, had little debt. Because in the past few decades, political reforms, order stabilization, and legal protection have been in place, the government has not paid attention to prevention, so the people's debt has deepened day by day. Indian courts enforce the law very quickly, and the government has detailed records of people's land registration in the land bureau. Lenders are willing to lend because they have protection, and people are willing to borrow because they lack education. When they encounter weddings and funerals, they borrow money from people, resulting in waste, so debt deepens day by day. In the past thirty years, with the cooperative movement, economic use, and proper allocation, there is now a need to borrow money in China. Because of frequent floods and droughts, as well as the increase in exorbitant taxes, people have an urgent need to borrow money. Also, although some farmers are poor, due to the import of foreign goods, the increase in machinery, and the high standard of living, people now have a demand and need for borrowing money, but lenders are unwilling to lend much, so the people's debt is not very heavy. Once politics is on track and those with money are willing to lend money, then the people's debt will inevitably become heavier day by day. Therefore, before the people's debt becomes heavy, there is one thing to pay attention to: (1) Find a way to have a good financial organization to facilitate circulation, while not causing the oppression of debt, that is, the need for the emergence of a credit cooperative system; (2) Improve production and marketing technology, that is, the need for the emergence of a marketing cooperative system; (3) Train people to know how to be frugal and how to allocate money for appropriate purposes, so as not to waste it. This can be guided by credit cooperatives and social improvement cooperatives. I hope that you will not only pay attention to the surface, but also pay attention to the content, and should find out the root cause and prescribe the right medicine. The root cause should also be explained in detail to farmers, and they should not only be given medicine to take. The above meaning may be difficult for ordinary farmers to understand, but you can agree that using charitable undertakings to help farmers will not have much effect. Because there are too many Chinese farmers, it is impossible to help them with charitable undertakings. They can only be trained to be self-reliant. Regarding charitable social organizations, farmers should be trained to manage their own businesses, and should not be placed under their guidance permanently. However, there is no need to operate too many businesses. The government should not use political coercion for reform undertakings, because the foundation cannot be sustained. China's future progress and the reform and upward movement of life cannot be achieved by government coercion. People must be willing to take this bright path. This requires a long period of education and guidance. Those who train cooperators should take on this responsibility, and they will be able to do it automatically in the future. The government should only use methods of persuasion and assistance, and the results will be great. It is extremely difficult for the government to have a relationship with every person, so there must be an organization. In India, every farmer has legitimate expenses and can borrow money from the government, but very few farmers borrow. This may also be the case in China, because people are afraid of having a relationship with the government, fearing danger. Egypt has an agricultural bank that can lend money to farmers, but after borrowing, they spend it all, and as a result, they sell land to repay the debt. China is also afraid of being in the same situation. There is only one way to make farmers have a group combination, mutually restrain and supervise each other, so as not to waste money. Several countries in the world lend money to farmers, not to individuals but to cooperatives. Commercial banks invest in rural areas. Siam, because it is a small country, directly lends money to cooperatives, but India, because it is a large country, can only lend to federations. China's area and population are roughly the same as India's, so it is best to lend to federations, which is more stable. If the amount of the loan is large, attention should be paid to whether the federation's loan to the cooperative is appropriate and whether its business operations are appropriate. Therefore, the bank should send specialists to the society to inspect. These people should have (1) knowledge of cooperation, (2) business training. The lack of either of these two conditions may cause danger to the bank's loan or to the farmers' business. Because farmers do not know how to keep accounts, and the inspectors themselves do not know it, the bank's investment will be in danger, and the farmers' share capital will also be lost. Not only knowledge of business methods, but also cooperation training is indispensable, otherwise they will not know how to allocate capital. If they do not know the principles of cooperation, they cannot proceed according to the principles of cooperation and will go astray, easily controlled by merchants. Therefore, those who actually guide cooperative work should pay attention to the principles of cooperation and business methods. Now I will talk about the definition of credit cooperation: (1) A credit cooperative is a combination of individuals; (2) The members within the cooperative are all on an equal footing; (3) The purpose is to obtain a kind of capital; (4) The capital can only circulate among the members; (5) The capital loan can only be used for beneficial purposes. There are two aspects to the foundation of credit cooperation, which the instructor should know, namely (1) the character of the members; (2) the management of the society's affairs. (End)

Chamber of Commerce Asks Ministry of Finance, Etc., to Order Courts to Accept Bonds as Security Deposit

Nationally Issued Bonds Are No Different from Cash

Court Refusal to Guarantee Bonds Has a Great Impact

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce yesterday submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Judicial Administration, stating that, "On the 19th of this month, the Timber Industry Association stated in a letter that the credit of national bonds or treasury bills should be stronger than any valuable securities. Therefore, the regulations for the issuance of national bonds or treasury bills clearly stipulate that they can be used as collateral for official guarantees, and it is often stated on the face of the bonds or treasury bills that no agency should refuse to provide guarantees. Unexpectedly, recently, some of our colleagues, when providing guarantees for litigation cases, based on the regulations of the national bonds and treasury bills, provided collateral, but were rejected by the Shanghai District Court and the Shanghai First Special District Court, saying that only cash guarantees were acceptable, which is not in accordance with the regulations of the bond regulations that can be provided for official guarantees, and it is detrimental to the credit of national bonds or treasury bills. Moreover, businesses have limited capital, and all commercial expenses and uses are causing turnover, how can they provide cash, restricting finance? The court's handling of this matter is particularly detrimental to business development. The Chamber of Commerce, in view of this, has specially written to your association to maintain commerce, that is, to request that the Ministry of Finance and Justice be forwarded to order all levels of courts across the country that if litigants provide guarantees with public debt treasury bills in the future, they should no longer refuse to force cash collection, so as to hinder public debt and maintain commerce, to hope for approval, and to quickly forward it, I am grateful, etc.," to the meeting. The national bonds treasury bills issued by the national government all have the following regulations in the regulations at the time of issuance: "This public debt or treasury bill can be used as a reserve fund for banks, and when other official duties require the payment of a security deposit, it can be used as collateral." The four characters of "other official duties" have a very broad meaning, and it seems that they cannot be interpreted as excluding official duties belonging to judicial events. Even according to the provisions of Article 102 of the current Civil Procedure Law, it states, "Those who provide guarantees shall deposit cash or valuable securities deemed appropriate by the court, but this does not apply if the parties have a special agreement." It is the current Civil Procedure Law that does not stipulate that guarantees must be cash. Moreover, the validity of nationally issued bonds and treasury bills circulating in the market is no different from cash, and their credit is far above ordinary valuable securities. According to the association's statement, it seems that the bonds provided by litigants as guarantees have been rejected by the courts, which makes the clause that bond regulations can be used as collateral for official duties almost a formality, which has a great impact on the circulation of national bonds. It is reasonable to report the situation and request that the Department of Justice review and approve the forwarding order to the courts, in accordance with the provisions of current laws and regulations, to accept and collect as usual, so as to maintain national debt credit, which is a public convenience. Respectfully submitted.

Salvation Army Scheduled to Fundraise

Enthusiastic Donors Can Send Donations to the North Suzhou Road Office

The Salvation Army has 90 agencies in China, from Shenyang in the north to Hong Kong in the south, with 263 staff members, the majority of whom are Chinese. The relief work it undertakes is the same for all, regardless of Chinese or foreign. It has a relief center for released prisoners in Shanghai. All Chinese who are released from the Huade Road Western Prison are given various assistance. Without the Salvation Army, these people would become homeless and helpless. In 1934, Salvation Army officers personally entered the prison and met with more than 11,200 Chinese prisoners. 499 of those who were released after serving their sentences were given travel expenses to return home, and some were given clothes, jobs were found for them, the sick were treated, and those without food were provided with three meals. A total of 1,548 new cotton-padded jackets were issued in one year. The Salvation Army is doing this in order to prevent these people from falling into despair and repeating their crimes, so as to benefit the city's security and order. It is planned to extend this work to the French Concession Chinese prison in the near future. As for the Huade Road Prison, Salvation Army officers often go there. Now, due to insufficient funds, it plans to start fundraising around March 1. This year's budget for relief work for Chinese and foreigners is 30,000 yuan. It is hoped that benevolent men and women will donate generously. Donations, no matter how large or small, can be sent to the Salvation Army Office at 422 North Suzhou Road.

Banking Industry Advocates Implementing International Exchange Management

Financial Advisory Committee Stabilizes Finance Initially

Ministry of Finance Plans to Levy Exchange Competitive Sales Tax

Dagon News reports, Since the Financial Advisory Committee organized by the Ministry of Finance was officially established on the 16th of this month at the Ministry of Finance's Shanghai Office on West Ames Road, its first step in planning to stabilize finance is to prepare to implement international exchange management methods. Regarding these methods, the banking industry and the committee have discussed the results, and the Banking Association has submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance to implement the collection of exchange rate competitive sales tax, in order to maintain the balance of international exchange and to serve as the foundation for stabilizing finance. A Dagon News reporter inquired about everything from the banking industry yesterday, and here is a detailed report.

Banking Industry Advocates According to a banking magnate, since Li Ming, General Manager of Zhejiang Industrial Bank, advocated exchange management, the general banking industry has expressed its approval. The Ministry of Finance's previous purpose in raising the silver tax was originally to cope with the temporary relief of the turmoil, which is not a permanent strategy for setting the price of silver. Moreover, the silver issue is not a simple monetary issue, but actually contains a relationship of commercial trade. Therefore, in order to absolutely prevent the outflow of silver, it is necessary to save imports. In order to save imports, it is necessary to stop the main source of imports. In recent years, the increase in China's imports has been due to the exchange rate competitive sales policies of various countries. Therefore, the banking industry generally believes that the Ministry of Finance should implement an exchange rate competitive sales tax.

Exchange Management Law As for the implementation of the exchange management law, the Financial Advisory Committee has predetermined three steps: (1) Exempt new silver imports from the equalization tax in order to absorb the input of foreign capital; (2) Maintain the current silver price, or raise it again, so as to maintain the balance between the domestic silver price and the foreign silver price; (3) If the United States still raises the silver price, formulate an exchange management law.

French Tram Company Robbed Yesterday Morning

Four Thousand Dollars Stolen, Fortunately No One Hurt

Robbers Fled Towards Route Conty Without a Trace

At 10:30 AM yesterday morning, at the intersection of Route Conty and Route LUBAN in the French Concession, the French-owned Water and Electricity Company was suddenly robbed by four bandits who opened fire and stole four thousand dollars. Fortunately, no one was injured. The robbers fled towards Route Conty without a trace. The details of the incident are as follows:

Escorting 20,000 Dollars

Tu Jinsheng, the comprador of the French-owned Water and Electricity Company in the French Concession, instructed Qin Rongsheng, a tea server from Changzhou in the company, to escort 20,000 dollars to the bank in the company's official car, license number 1328 in the French Concession and 1886 in the Chinese area, at 10:30 AM yesterday morning. Beforehand, the company's office divided this large sum of 20,000 dollars into two canvas bags, one containing 16,000 dollars in banknotes and the other containing 2,000 dollars in silver coins and 2,000 dollars in banknotes. No sooner had the car driven out of the company gate than

Four Robbers

who seemed to have been lying in wait for a long time, immediately drew their pistols. Two robbers stopped the car, and two robbers rushed into the car and snatched one bag containing 4,000 dollars. Qin Rongsheng, the tea server escorting the money, seeing the situation was bad, quickly threw the remaining bag into the company gate from the car. In their haste, the robbers did not have time to rob again, so they fired two shots into the air as a warning, and then boarded a white-牌 car that had been parked by the side of the road. They forced the driver out and drove the car themselves towards Route Conty

and sped away.

The reporter from the Guowen News Agency arrived at the scene of the incident around 11:00 AM and saw a large number of detectives dispatched by the French Concession Police Station still lingering in the company. They had also taken the driver who had been forced out of the car to the police station for questioning. According to him, his name was Luo Zhixiang, and he was a driver for the Haoyou Automobile Company at 112 Guangxi Road. At 9:30 AM this morning (i.e., yesterday), two young male customers suddenly

Called for a Car

and specified that they wanted to go to Route LUBAN in the French Concession for a round trip fare of two dollars. I (Luo claiming himself) was dispatched to drive a brown sedan, French Concession license number 17625 and Chinese Concession license number 4574. When we reached the intersection of Route LUBAN and Ximen Road, two more people got into the car by the side of the road. I continued to drive to the front of the tram company and parked. One of them told me to wait a moment. I saw all four customers go inside. Not a moment later, I suddenly heard gunshots. I was in a state of panic when one of the customers suddenly approached me,

Drew a Pistol

and forced me out. Because the matter was so sudden, I stood in front of a cigarette shop and waited. After the original car was driven away by the four customers, I was about to report to the police when the police detectives arrived. I was arrested," etc. After the reporter left the police station, he went to the tram company to inquire. According to them, they knew nothing about it beforehand. The company's bodyguards heard the sound and ran out, immediately drawing their guns and waiting in front of the comprador's office on the right side of the second gate. They wanted to chase after the robbers, but unexpectedly, the machinery suddenly malfunctioned, so they did not dare to chase out of the gate. The robbers escaped calmly. The tea server, Qin Rongsheng, took the remaining bag back. Upon inspection, the 16,000 dollars in cash was

Still Safe and Sound

After the incident, the company reported to the police station and requested a search. However, according to a person from a nearby cigarette shop, there were more than two gunshots. Everyone was afraid to look out. After a while, they saw a red car speeding away and turning towards Route Conty. There was a traffic police officer there who was in charge of the traffic lights, but at that time, he did not know what was going on, so even though he had a gun in his hand, he did not dare to open fire easily, allowing the robbers to escape.

Telephone Company's Request to Increase Prices

Published by the Public Information Office of the Municipal Council

The Shanghai Telephone Company's application to revise the rate schedule has been preliminarily considered by the Public Utilities Committee of the Municipal Council. The committee's record was submitted to the Board of Directors for review yesterday (Wednesday). The company's request aims to increase total revenue by 22.89% in order to obtain interest as stipulated in the concession contract (of which 2% is to be used as a general reserve fund). According to Article 13 of the new concession contract signed between the Municipal Council and the company on August 5, 1930, after the completion of the automatic machine conversion, the company should have a net profit income of 8%, plus 2% as a reserve fund. However, it was also agreed that the rate schedule should not exceed the amount recommended in the Anson report within the first three years. The automatic machine conversion was completed on March 27, 1932. Since then, the Municipal Council has approved the collection of fees according to the Anson rate schedule. However, in August 1933, the company requested a revision of the rate schedule due to the discovery of unforeseen circumstances. The Municipal Council then provided financial assistance to resolve the difficulties. At the same time, the company acknowledged that (1) the amount of the price increase should not exceed 25% from April 1, 1935, (2) no further increase should be made before March 1937, and that the contract should be followed thereafter, and (3) if the income exceeds 10% of the capital from April 1, 1935, to March 31, 1937, the contract should be followed. If there is a shortfall, it should be entered under the rate revision account and made up after March 1937. The company claims that it has made every effort to streamline construction and operations without affecting the scope of services. However, the income in 1934 only reached 6.13% of the capital amount. In order to reach the annual profit of 8% plus 2% stipulated in the contract, it is necessary to increase the company's total revenue by 22.89% from April 1, 1935. This increase can be achieved in two ways: one is to universally increase the user's bills by this percentage, and the other is to adopt the principle of charging per call to distribute the cost of telephone calls more fairly. The company believes that the second method is more economical and reasonable, at least for business telephones. In smaller cities, it is sufficient to set a fixed rate for business telephones that is slightly higher than that for residential telephones. However, in large cities, this method makes large users much cheaper, while small users suffer a lot. The fixed rate charging method is easy to cause excessive calls in large cities. As a result, the company's consumption will inevitably increase, and not only is there unlimited calls between users, but there is also no limit to the matter of borrowing telephone calls. As a result, the company's income is lost and expenses are increased. The company's opinion is that residential telephones in Shanghai can temporarily continue to use the fixed rate charging method, while business telephones must be charged according to the number of calls recorded by the register. In 1931, before the automatic machine was converted, the average number of calls per line per day was 7.12 times. Last year, it increased to 14.81 times. The burden on the machine is often very heavy. If it is abused without restriction, the company will have to add another 3.5 million yuan of capital to increase equipment. As for the company's proposed rate revision methods, they are listed below: 1. The original monthly rate for business telephones is reduced from a fixed rate of 12.24 yuan to 10 yuan, limited to 100 calls. After this number, the rate is proportionally reduced, with a minimum of 3 cents per call. This can increase total revenue by 16.488%. 2. The fixed monthly rate for residential telephones is increased from 7.58 yuan to 8.50 yuan, which can increase total revenue by 2.613%. 3. Private lines are calculated based on aerial lines instead of ground lines, and the rates are proportional, which can increase total revenue by 2.579%. 4. The original per-call rate for business telephones is also changed to the first method, which can increase total revenue by 1.545%. 5. The switchboard fee is reduced from 1.47 yuan per month to 1 yuan, which reduces total revenue by 1.429%. 6. The installation and relocation fee is changed from 13.99 yuan to 15 yuan for business use and 10 yuan for residential use, which has no impact on total revenue. 7. The original rate for extension and extension telephones is 2.10 yuan per unit, which is reduced proportionally for more units. Now it is changed to a uniform 2 yuan, which increases total revenue by 0.662%. 8. The private branch exchange is increased by 26.5% to 100% depending on its size, which increases total revenue by 0.461%. 9. The reconnection fee is changed from the original 2.80 yuan to 2 yuan, which reduces total revenue by 0.029%. After the above methods are added and subtracted, the total revenue can be increased by 22.89%. According to the first method, businesses that make fewer calls can pay less than they do now. It is hoped that the number of new users will increase. Also, according to the new method, income and expenses can be adjusted in tandem. In this way, the calculation method of telephone charges can avoid constant changes. Judging from the experience of other places, the number of business telephone calls can be reduced by 50% within two or three years after the implementation of the new method. The burden on those who make the most calls will be greatly increased, but for 65% of users, the price increase will not exceed 15%. The development of housing is still very low in Shanghai, so the price of residential telephones is still kept as low as possible. The various changes proposed by Wang Others are only intended to make the cost of telephone calls more even. According to the company's calculations, after the proposed new method is implemented, an income of about 10.08% of the investment amount can be obtained annually within two years, but it still depends on the development of the entire telephone system and the number of calls. The company also cites the construction and operating costs of other companies for comparison, and the expenses of the Shanghai Telephone Company are not high.

Notorious Thief Zhou Maoxian Executed by Hanging Yesterday

Hoped to Write to Family to Take Care of Old Mother

Face Pale, Looked Remorseful

The notorious thief Zhou Maoxian, 49 years old, from Yancheng, was sentenced to death for leading a gang armed with weapons at 7:40 AM on December 3 of the year before last to rob the family property of Mrs. Zhou Yi at 4 Huatongfang, North Xizang Road, and fleeing. When Chinese and Western detectives from the police station arrived to arrest them, the accomplices fled in a hurry from the Manzhou Road area of Zhabei. Police officer Zhang Liankui, number 2073 of the Public Security Bureau, tried to stop them, but he opened fire and refused to be arrested, hitting a vital point and seriously injuring him. He died after ineffective treatment. Later, Chinese and Western detectives from the Hongkou police station found Zhou in the Linchun Tea House on Jiujiang Road, arrested him, and escorted him to the First Special District Court. After a clear confession, he was sentenced to death, which was approved by the Jiangsu Provincial Government and ordered to be executed. Yesterday morning, the police took Zhou from prison and sent him to the Third Criminal Court. He asked to send two letters, one to his brother-in-law Yin Si at the thatched cottage west of the milk shed on Jiangwan Road in Shanghai, and the other to Wang Kaiyuan, the owner of the tiger stove in Zhangjia Lane, north of Xiangyan Bridge, to be forwarded to his cousin Hu Da and two sisters, asking them to take care of his mother. When he was arrested, he had dozens of copper coins with him, which he wanted to use to buy long ingots for burning. He said that it would be best if his sisters were willing to go to the execution ground to collect his body, otherwise they could do as they pleased. When he spoke, his face was pale and he looked remorseful. The court ordered the Chinese and Western police to take him down and announced that Zhou Maoxian was to be handed over to the Shanghai Local Court Prosecutor's Office for execution by hanging in accordance with the law. He was then escorted along with the entire case file and portrait, and driven to the execution ground of the Second Prison in Caohejing. The prosecutor arrived at the scene to identify Zhou and ordered the judicial police to tie him up and execute him in accordance with the law. According to the law, the body was exposed overnight, and the coffin was collected by the hall the next day.

Mahjong Gambling Scam

The Backs of the Tiles All Had Secret Marks

Mrs. Chen Suffered Heavy Losses

—False Report of Robbery Led to the Discovery—

The day before yesterday afternoon, as dawn was breaking, at around 4:00 AM, the Laozha Police Station received a report from Wang Mingde, stating that there were robbers holding weapons and robbing at the Xin Inn at the intersection of Hubei Road and Jiujiang Road, and requesting an investigation. The police chief, upon receiving the report, immediately ordered Western Detective Translator, Chinese Detective Li Shugui, and Patrol Detectives Yang Guanying and Sun Dafa to go there with weapons. According to the report, the robbers were in the corridor in the courtyard. The Chinese and Western detectives saw several people trying to escape and ordered them to stop, but they did not listen. Western Detective Translator then fired a shot as a warning, fortunately without injuring anyone. Later, Chen Axin and Ding Haikang were arrested in the urinal. A mahjong set and a deck of poker cards with secret marks were found on Ding's person. Shao Laishun was also arrested and taken to the police station. After investigation, it was discovered that this case was not a robbery, but a gambling scam to defraud money. Subsequently, gambling offenders Wang Mingde, Yuan Qiaofu, Chen Xushi, Yang Chenshi, Zhou Houfu, Zhou Huaqing, Chen Guitang, Zhang Bingrong, Zhou Huaxiang, Yang Xinlong, Li Jiazhuang, Yang Xieshi, Chen Jinmei, Xu Chenshi, Zhang Liushi (i.e., A Mei), Wang Chenshi, and Chen Weishi, along with the previous Chen Axin and others, for a total of 20 people, were arrested. Among them, Shao Laishun was used as a witness, and the remaining 19 people, including women, were prosecuted for fraud and gambling. It was also found that the group had colluded to defraud Mrs. Chen Ayu of 582 yuan with mahjong tiles with secret marks. It turned out that Mrs. Chen Ayu, a woman from Ningbo, was now 23 years old. She had once been a prostitute in a Ningbo brothel. After becoming a respectable woman, she followed her husband to Ningbo. This time, she came to Shanghai from her hometown on the 11th of this month and opened a room at the Huizhong Xin Inn on Hankou Road. On the 14th, she met her old friend, Mrs. Zhang Liushi, i.e., A Mei, and invited her to her house at 25, Lane 117, Shandong Road, to reminisce about old times. (It was found that Zhang A Mei had been running a Ningbo brothel in Room 136 of the Xin Inn.) Before long, they began to play mahjong. After eight rounds, it was midnight. Zhang saw that Chen Ayu was wealthy and assumed that she had a lot of money, so she invited Chen to Room 126 of the Xin Inn. At that time, there were already people in a room opposite gambling mahjong. Zhang's mother also obtained Chen's consent to join the game and asked Chen to be the banker, while Zhang Liushi joined the stake for a quarter. Chen did not know that there was a scam, and the backs of the tiles all had secret marks, so at the end of one round, Chen lost 220 yuan. After that, she went gambling from time to time, losing badly a total of three times. The second time she lost 225 yuan, and the third time she lost 137 yuan, for a total of 580 yuan. Until the night before last, someone secretly told Chen about the scam. Chen knew that she had been cheated, so she went to Room 261 of the Xin Inn at night to visit Shao Laishun and others, and invited Qiu Yongyu and others to reason with Zhang Liushi, ordering her to hand over the mahjong tiles. Zhang not only refused, but also accused Shao of damaging her reputation and trying to extort 500 yuan. They then began to quarrel and even fight. At the same time, Wang Mingde falsely reported a robbery, which led to the above incident. Yesterday morning, the police escorted the criminals to the Second Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Police lawyer Zhang Shizhu stated the above situation and said that there was still extortion in this case, so he requested permission to reschedule the hearing. He then presented the dice and mahjong tiles. Subsequently, Chen Ayu and witness Shao Laishun filed a complaint about the previous situation. After interrogating each of the defendants, Judge Ye Shengchao ordered Wang Mingde, Yang Chenshi, and Zhang Liushi to be detained, and the others were released on bail of 50 yuan each, pending a rescheduled hearing next Monday.

Salvation of Beggars Association Sends Letter to Municipal Public Security Bureau Requesting Assistance in Sheltering Female Beggars

Directly Send to Hospital for Care to Avoid Complications

Temporarily Suspended Sheltering of Child Beggars to Raise Funds for New Building

The Salvation of Beggars Association, sponsored by the Chinese Women's Temperance Association, has been working hard to shelter women and children beggars since its establishment. It is learned that the Association, in order to expand its shelter, yesterday sent a letter to the Municipal Public Security Bureau requesting the arrest of female beggars and sending them to the shelter. However, because the number of child beggars and young children carried by beggar women has reached its maximum, the shelter has temporarily suspended sheltering. It is now raising funds to establish a nursery so that they can be accommodated. The details are as follows:

Letter to Municipal Public Security Bureau

The Association sent a letter to the Municipal Public Security Bureau yesterday, which stated, "Sir, we previously received your letter in which you agreed to order your subordinates to assist us as much as possible in sheltering beggars, for which we are very grateful. The Association now reports that the children's department is full. Once funds are raised and a nursery is built in the future, we will carry out a large-scale shelter. We are now planning to shelter and care for single female beggars in the Jiangwan, Nanshi, Zhabei, and other areas. We urge your bureau to order your subordinates to directly send these female beggars to the Shanghai Women and Children's Education and Care Institute on Xiangyin Road, Jiangwan, starting next week, to avoid complications. We hope for your assistance."

Planned Construction of Nursery

According to Liu Wang Liming, director of the Association, since the establishment of the Association to shelter women and children beggars, there have been many people outside who have voluntarily requested shelter, but there must also be many people who have not been sheltered because they do not know the location or the location of the shelter. However, the Association is only run by a small number of women, and it is deeply regrettable that it has not been able to shelter as much as possible sooner due to limited financial resources. The Association has temporarily suspended sheltering due to the full capacity of child beggars. It is now planning to find ways to raise funds to build a larger nursery so that it can shelter as many child beggars as possible.

Jailers Charged in Murderer's Jailbreak Case

Suspected of Facilitating Escape

Brought Before the Court for Questioning Yesterday

Murderer Chen Jinlan, a native of Yong, 32 years old, was arrested by detectives from the French police in a rural area of Ningbo for shooting and killing Chen Zhikui, the young owner of Qianfengtai Incense Candle Shop, number 52 Dongxinqiao Street, French Concession, on the evening of April 14, 1933. She was extradited to Shanghai and prosecuted by the Second Special District Court. After three trials by the Supreme Court, she was sentenced to 12 years in prison. Chen was detained in cell number 11, East Section, of the Second Special District Court Detention Center during the appeal period and was about to be executed. However, Chen miraculously escaped without a trace between 3:00 AM and 7:00 AM on December 27 of last year. It was not until the cell was opened at 7:10 AM that the guards discovered the escape and reported it to the warden, Gao Xiaoge. The six guards on duty, Yang Xingcun, Wang Guanghe, Fang Yuqi, Han Haorui, Yan Ling, and Zhou Wenjin, were detained and transferred to the Prosecutor's Office of the Second Special District Court for investigation. At the same time, the Gao Third Sub-court Prosecutor's Office was requested to issue an arrest warrant for the fugitive Chen Jinlan. Details have been reported in previous newspapers. This case has been repeatedly investigated by Prosecutor Wang Ren, and witnesses Cai Qinquan, Bai Zengqing, prison staff Zou Lusheng, and Yu Decai have been summoned to the case. After the interrogation and investigation were completed, it was determined that Fang Yuqi (40 years old, from Anhui), the cell guard on duty, and Zhou Wenjin (19 years old, from Hebei), the guard at the main gate and rear iron gate, had neglected their duties and were suspected of facilitating the escape. Therefore, Chen and the two guards, Fang and Zhou, were prosecuted to the same-level court in accordance with Articles 170 and 172 of the Criminal Code. The four guards, Yang, Wang, Han, and Yan, who were found to be unrelated to the case, were ordered to be released on bail and returned to the detention center to serve. Yesterday, Judge Zhang Chaozuo of the Criminal Court of the Second Special District Court specially opened the Fifth Court and ordered the defendants Fang Yuqi and Zhou Wenjin, who were in custody, to be brought in, and summoned witnesses Bai Zengqing, Cai Qinquan, Yang Xingcun, Yan Ling, Zou Lusheng, and Yu Decai, the director and deputy director of the detention center, and guards, to the court for questioning. Fang and Zhou had lawyers Ting Zhu Dianqing and others to defend them. The testimonies of the defendants and witnesses were the same as those in the investigation court. They will not be repeated here. The questioning lasted for one and a half hours before it ended. The court ordered the defendants to be returned to custody, and the witnesses were dismissed to await a scheduled hearing.

Six Bodies Verified in Deng Tuo Road Fire

Cause of Fire Under Investigation

On Deng Tuo Road, Deng Tuo Lane, 28 ½ Dai Fu Lane, a fire suddenly broke out at about 2:00 AM the day before yesterday. At that time, the entire houses of 28 ½ and 29 ½ were burned down, and the roofs of 27, 28, and 29 were burned. Six men, women, and children were burned to death on the spot (all residents of 28 ½) and two men were injured. The injured men were residents of 29 ½. After the fire brigade heard the alarm, they immediately went to the scene with Chinese and Western detectives from the Huishan Police Station to put out the fire. After two hours, the fire was extinguished and the dead and injured were sent to the hospital and morgue. It has been reported in this newspaper. It is learned that Detective Li Zhaogeng of the police station has identified the deceased as Zheng Lao Liu, 30 years old, from Jiangbei, residing on the second floor; Tang Er Mazi, 21 years old, and Tang Zhongshi, 18 years old, from Tongzhou, residing in the back hall, a married couple, and a boy who had just been born for more than a month; Li Wentian, 54 years old, and his wife Zhao, 53 years old, residing in the front building. The injured were Tao Han, 30 years old, from Chongming, and Chou Guiyuan, 39 years old, from Anhui. Yesterday morning, the First Special District Court appointed Prosecutor Guo Wei and Doctors Wei and Zhang, as well as Secretary Wang Zuyi, to go to the morgue to verify the bodies. The Western police chief reported the previous situation and said that the fire started at 28 ½, and there were as many as 15 people living in the house. As for the cause of the fire, it is still under investigation. The families of the deceased have all arrived. Prosecutor Guo then briefly questioned the families and announced that the deceased men Li Wentian, Zheng Lao Liu, Tang Er Mazi, and the boy, and the women Li Zhao and Tang Zhongshi, had all been burned to death. The bodies of Li Wentian and Li Zhao were handed over to Cui Guangren, the body of Zheng Lao Liu was handed over to Liu Zhengqiu, and the bodies of Tang Er Mazi, Tang Zhongshi, and the boy were handed over to Tang San for separate collection and burial.

Conspiracy to Bomb the Shun'an Steamer—Three Bottles of Liquid Tested; Results Now Available

The test results show it was not explosives, but rather refrigeration oil.

Confirmed by Ouyang Tai to be the original items from Chen Youbai.

The Shun'an steamer, owned by the Shun'an Steamer Company, traveling between Shanghai and Xinghua, Fujian, last autumn, loaded goods in Shanghai and set sail for Fujian. When it reached Sanduwo in Fujian, the ship owner Ouyang Tai suddenly reported to the local customs, claiming that the company manager, Chen Youbai, secretly instructed to destroy the ship mid-voyage in order to fraudulently obtain insurance compensation. Unwilling to see the lives of the entire ship sacrificed innocently, he reported the information. After receiving the report, the customs, considering the seriousness of the matter, immediately ordered the ship to be detained, and Ouyang Tai was escorted to the Minhou District Court in Fujian for interrogation and detention. Meanwhile, the company's chairman, Zheng Zhongwu, learned of the situation and reported it to the authorities. Chen Youbai was arrested and handed over to the Second Special District Court. Due to jurisdictional issues, the case fell under the jurisdiction of the Nanshi District Court, so Chen Youbai was transferred to the District Court. At the same time, police were dispatched to the Minhou District Court in Fujian to bring Ouyang Tai back to Shanghai. After clear interrogation, the case was prosecuted in the Criminal Division and has been opened for trial three times.

Due to the complexity of the case,

it has not yet concluded. Details have been previously reported. It is now known that the case was re-tried yesterday at 10:00 AM by Judge Liu Enrong of the Criminal Division (the original trial judge was Chen Jingyi). After the judge took the bench, he ordered Ouyang Tai, who was in custody, to be brought to the stand. Ouyang Tai stated that he was 32 years old, from Fujian, and served as the owner of the Shun'an steamer. He was asked when the Shun'an steamer departed for Xinghua, Fujian. He replied that it was on September 13th of last year at 5:00 AM, departing from Shanghai. He was asked what kind of goods the Shun'an steamer was carrying. He replied that it was carrying soybean cakes, tea, cloth, and the like. He was asked what the tonnage of the Shun'an steamer was. He replied that it was around 1,350 tons. He was asked where he reported the matter. He replied that it was at Sanduwo Customs. He was asked whether he reported it himself or if someone else did it on his behalf. He replied that he went to report it to the Customs Commissioner himself. He was asked to

briefly describe

the situation he reported to the customs. Ouyang replied that around 7:00 AM on September 10th of last year, Chen Youbai came to his house to meet and said, "When the ship sails this time, you must run the ship aground. I have already made arrangements with the customs broker to falsely report that we are carrying 29,722 pieces of cargo. If the ship encounters danger, we can get more than 100,000 yuan in insurance money. Then we can buy a bigger ship, and you can still be the ship owner, and I will give you an insurance policy worth 4,800 yuan as a reward." (The insurance policy had already been filed.) "If you leak the news, I will take your life." On the 12th, he urged him to go to the fifth floor of the Yangtze Hotel to discuss destroying the ship again. In the evening, he was invited to a banquet at the Huichuan Shipping Company. After the banquet, he accompanied him to the Yangtze Hotel and gave him three bottles of explosive liquid. At that time, he vaguely agreed. On the 13th, the ship set sail. When the ship sailed outside the Wusong port, Zheng A'kang, the brother of Chairman Zheng Zhongwu, was on the ship, forcing him to blow up the ship and calling a

meeting of the crew

to have Shan A'kang take responsibility after the ship encountered danger and to allocate one year's salary to each person on the ship. He strongly opposed it at the time. He immediately ordered the telegraph operator to send a telegram to report to the Shanghai Customs, but Zheng A'kang stepped in to stop it. However, the crew knew about the plot to blow up the ship, so when the ship arrived at Sanduwo, he reported the information to the Customs Commissioner. He was asked what evidence he had of Chen Youbai contacting him about blowing up the ship. He replied that the contact was verbal and that he was given an insurance policy worth 4,800 yuan as proof. The judge ordered Chen Youbai to come to the stand. Chen Youbai stated that he was 35 years old and was the manager of the Shun'an Steamer Company. He was asked what he managed. He replied that business transactions and customs declarations were all handled by him. He was asked whether he managed the ship's destination. He replied that it was under the command of the general manager, Zheng Zhongwu. He was asked how much cargo was loaded this time. He replied that it was over 14,000 pieces. He was asked

why he falsely reported

29,722 pieces. He was asked the reason. He replied that the remaining pieces had already been cleared from customs. He was asked, according to the customs, the goods were not cleared, and they did not allow him to clear them. He replied that the customs had already cleared them. If they had not been cleared, the Xinghua Customs would have to detain their ship. He was asked if he knew that the ship was detained in Sanduwo. He replied that he only found out on the 18th. He was asked how long Ouyang Tai had been the ship owner. He replied that he had previously served as the ship owner for three months at the company. Now, he was recommended by Zheng Zhongwu to continue serving as the ship owner. He was asked if Ouyang Tai had any grudges against him. He replied that he had previously suspended him from his position, so he inevitably held a grudge, and their relationship was not very harmonious. He was asked if the three bottles of explosive liquid and the insurance policy worth 4,800 yuan were given to Ouyang Tai by him. He replied that he did not. He was asked if the crew also said that he contacted Ouyang Tai about blowing up the ship. He replied that the crew were subordinates of Ouyang. The interrogating judge said to Chen, "Ouyang Tai earns over 200 yuan a month. Now he is

sacrificing his position

and still suffering. He is not crazy. If you did not contact Ouyang Tai, would he have gone to report to the Sanduwo Customs?" Chen's reply was ambiguous. Next, Zheng A'kang was brought to the stand. He stated that he was 20 years old and currently studying. He was asked if he had a position on the Shun'an steamer. He replied that he did not. He was asked what he was doing on the ship. He replied that he was returning to his hometown to take care of his father's funeral. He was asked if he knew about Ouyang's contact about blowing up the ship. He replied that he only found out when he got on the ship. He was asked how he knew. He replied that the old shipmate told him. He was asked why the old shipmate told him. He replied that when the ship was sailing, he was bored and casually looking around and passed by the ship owner's room and saw many crew members inside talking. When they saw him coming, they were all silent and dispersed. He was asked where he went when he arrived at Sanduwo. He replied that he went to the naval department to report the information to Battalion Commander Li. The next day (i.e., the 16th), he

telegraphed Shanghai

to his brother Zheng Zhongwu. He was asked if Ouyang Tai and crew members Lin Xifan and Wang Jixin all said that he forced Ouyang to blow up the ship. Zheng replied that this was not the case. At this point in the interrogation, Judge Liu ordered the forensic doctor to come to the court to testify. After testing the three bottles of explosive liquid presented in the case, the results showed that it was not explosives, but rather something like refrigeration oil. Judge Liu ordered Ouyang Tai to come to the stand to inspect the three bottles of explosive liquid presented in the case. He was asked if they were the original items. Ouyang inspected them for a long time and replied that they were, in fact, the original items given to him by Chen Youbai. At this point in the interrogation, Judge Liu stated that the circumstances of the case were extremely complicated, and further investigation and witness examination were necessary. The hearing would be continued at a later date. The defendants Chen Youbai and Zheng A'kang were released on their original bail, while Ouyang Tai was remanded in custody pending further instructions.

Bizarre Incident in Tangqiao, Pudong: Disinterring Graves and Whipping Corpses on Public Cemetery Land

Heads of the Dead Displayed—a Chilling Sight for Onlookers

The Purpose Is Simply to Hold a Festival to Welcome the Gods

—We Urge the Authorities to Investigate Thoroughly—

Hua Dong News Agency: A ridiculous and bizarre movement has recently occurred in Pudong. The absurdity and cruelty of the event are no different from the actions of primitive barbarian tribes. The incident took place in Tangqiao Township, which is also under the jurisdiction of Shanghai. The instigators were a group of local ruffians. Ignorant villagers blindly followed. The purpose was to promote festival activities in the countryside. The first day of the movement was the evening of the 18th of this month, which was also the Lantern Festival according to the lunar calendar. At 8:30 PM that night, several hooligans suddenly went to the Zhaotianhou Temple in the eastern town of the township and carried out a small statue of the god Zhaotianhou enshrined in the temple. This small statue is used as a pioneer during the festival parades. Immediately, a group of people were gathered, holding torches, and went to the public cemetery about a mile away from the town, called "running the altar." They shouted loudly on the cemetery, their behavior resembling the attendants shouting in the officialdom during the Qing Dynasty, called "calling the hall." After the "calling the hall" was completed, they arbitrarily split the unclaimed coffins of newly deceased people on the cemetery and forcibly removed the heads of the corpses and hung them on the chair of the small statue. According to witnesses, the scene was extremely tragic and difficult to describe. Last night was the second night of "running the altar." They went even further to the public cemetery two miles away from the town and carried out the same actions. The mentality of this group of inhuman people is even more laughable. It is said that collecting a large number of dead people's heads can promote the early spiritual response of the Bodhisattva. Only in this way can the sponsorship of local gentry be promoted by the Bodhisattva's response, and the festival activities can be held as scheduled. Since this incident occurred, a large number of ignorant villagers have followed suit. As a result, the township has been disturbed all night for consecutive nights, and strange incidents abound. The Tangqiao Road Police Station of the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau is located in the Tianzhu Temple. The hooligans are afraid of being discovered by the police station, so their actions were very secretive when carrying out the small statue. However, since the movement occurred, the unclaimed coffins in the public cemetery have suffered tragic mutilation after death. It is sincerely hoped that the authorities will quickly stop this absurd act and strictly investigate the ringleaders, so that this barbaric and inhuman phenomenon can gradually subside.

Soviet International Film Festival Representatives Zhou Jianyun and Hu Die to Depart Today

Accompanied by Mr. and Mrs. Yan Mei

Zhou Jianyun and Hu Die, the representatives of our country to the Soviet International Film Exhibition, have been extremely busy with preparations since their itinerary was decided. In addition to Zhou and Hu's friends giving farewell banquets one after another, the colleagues of the Star Film Company held a farewell meeting at 3:00 PM yesterday afternoon. Huangshan Construction Funding Custody and Audit Committees Established

Yang Hu and Others Appointed as Committee Members

A Joint Meeting Was Held Yesterday

In order to ensure the proper use of funds, the Huangshan Construction Committee established the Construction Funding Custody and Audit Committees the day before yesterday. Yang Hu and others were appointed as committee members, and the detailed rules of procedure were adopted, as follows:

Appointment of Committee Members

The Huangshan Construction Committee held a general meeting for the establishment of the Custody and Audit Committees at its office on Luban Road at 3:00 PM the day before yesterday afternoon. Chairman Xu Shiying presided over the meeting and appointed Yang Hu, the director of the Municipal Security Bureau, Supervisory Committee members Gao Yihan, Wang Zhongqi, Wu Dieqing, Xu Jiqing, Hong Yulin, Xu Jingren, Guan Yunnong, Jiang Tonghou, and other committee members.

Adoption of Detailed Rules

The Detailed Rules of Procedure for the Construction Funding Custody and Audit Committees of the Huangshan Construction Committee are as follows: (1) These two committees shall formulate detailed rules of procedure in accordance with Article 5 of the Huangshan Construction Committee Organization Charter. (2) The Custody Committee shall mutually elect two to three members to be responsible for managing the deposit and withdrawal of funds. When depositing and withdrawing funds, one or two committee members must sign and seal the documents. (3) The Audit Committee shall mutually elect two or three members to be responsible for auditing the use of funds. (4) The Custody Committee shall hold meetings in January and July each year to prepare a statement of income and expenditure, which shall be distributed to the Standing Committee and the Audit Committee. (5) The Audit Committee shall hold meetings in February and August each year to audit the budget of payments, statement of payments, and statement of income and expenditure prepared by the Standing Committee. (6) The Standing Committee may convene temporary meetings of the Custody and Audit Committees when necessary. (7) When the Custody and Audit Committees need personnel to handle affairs, they may temporarily transfer personnel from the Huangshan Construction Committee's Shanghai Office and Nanjing Information Office. (8) These detailed rules shall be implemented upon the decision of the joint meeting of the Custody and Audit Committees. If there are any omissions, they may be amended upon the proposal of three or more committee members.

Joint Meeting

At 3:00 PM yesterday afternoon, the committee held its second joint meeting, attended by Xu Shiying, Yang Hu, Gao Yihan, Hong Yiwo, Guan Yunnong, Xu Jingren, Wang Zhongqi, Huang Binhong, Huang Bonongdu, and others. Xu Shiying was elected as the chairman of the meeting. It was decided at the meeting to sign the regulations separately, and the meeting adjourned around 4:00 PM.
